pataye ca eva bhūtānām pataye namaḥ praṇane ṛk yajuḥ sāmne svadhāyai ca sudhāya ca vaṣaṭkāra tamāya eva tubhyam anta ātmane namaḥ sraṣṭre dhātre tathā hotre hartre ca kṣapaṇāya ca vasave ca eva sādhyāya rudra āditya aśvināya ca dakṣiṇa avabhṛthāya eva tubhyam yajña ātmane namaḥ ahiṃsāya api alobhāya su veśāya atiśāya ca sarva bhūta ātma bhūtāya tubhyam yoga ātmane namaḥ pṛthivyai ca antarikṣāya divāya ca mahāya ca tanmātrāya mahāntāya tubhyam tattva ātmane namaḥ nityāya ca artha liṅgāya sūkṣmāya cetanāya ca namaḥ te triṣu lokeṣu svara anteṣu bhava ādiṣu evam ārādhya deveśam īśānam nīlalohitam kāvyasya gātram saṃspṛśya hastena prītimān bhavaḥ nikāmam darśanam dattvā tatra eva antaradhīyata tiṣṭhantīm prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā jayantīm idam abravīt kasya tvam subhage kā vā duḥkhite mayi duḥkhitā mahatā tapasā yuktam kimartham mān jugopasi evam uktā tapasā jñātum arhasi cikīrṣitam me brahniṣṭha tvam hi vettha yathātatham evam ukte abravīt enām dṛṣṭvā divyena cakṣuṣā māhendrī tvam varārohe mad hita artham iha āgatā mayā saha tvam suśroṇi daśa varṣāṇi bhāmini imam vṛṇīṣva kāmam te mattaḥ vai valgu bhāṣiṇi evam bhavatu gacchāmaḥ gṛhān vai mattakāśini sa tayā sam sat devyā daśa varṣāṇi bhāgaśas adṛśyaḥ sarva bhūtānām māyayā saṃvṛtaḥ tadā kṛtārtham āgatam dṛṣṭvā kāvyam sarve diteḥ sutāḥ abhijagmuḥ gṛham tasya muditāḥ te didṛkṣavaḥ gatāḥ yadā na paśyantaḥ jayantyā saṃvṛtam gurum bṛhaspatiḥ tu saṃruddham jñātvā kāvyam cakāra ha pitṛ arthe daśa varṣāṇi jayantyā hita kāmyayā kāvyasya rūpam āsthāya saḥ asurān samabhāṣata tatas samāgatān dṛṣṭvā bṛhaspatiḥ uvāca tān svāgatam mama yājyānām saṃprāptaḥ asmi hitāya ca aham vaḥ adhyāpayiṣyāmi prāptā vidyā mayā hi sā pūrṇakāmaḥ tadā tasmin samaye daśa vārṣike buddhim cakre tatas ca api yājyānām pratyavekṣaṇe devi gacchāmahe draṣṭum tava yājyān śuci smite tatas gatvā asurān dṛṣṭvā devācāryeṇa dhīmatā vāñcitān kāvya rūpeṇa vedhasā asuram abravīt vañcitāḥ bata yūyam vai mayi śakte tu dānavāḥ śrutvā tathā bruvāṇantam sambhrāntāḥ ditijāḥ tatas sampramūḍhāḥ sthitāḥ sarve prāpadyanta na kiñcana tatas teṣu pramūḍheṣu kāvyaḥ tān punar abravīt ācāryyaḥ vaḥ hi aham kāvyaḥ deva ācāryaḥ ayam aṅgirāḥ tadā asurāḥ na vyajānan tayoḥ dvayoḥ bṛhaspatiḥ uvāca etān asambhrāntaḥ ayam aṅgirāḥ kāvyaḥ aham yaḥ guruḥ daityāḥ mad rūpaḥ ayam bṛhaspatiḥ sa mohayati rūpeṇa māmakena eṣa vaḥ asurāḥ ayan naḥ daśa varṣāṇi satatam śāsti vai prabhuḥ tatas te dānavāḥ sarve praṇipatya abhivādya ca vacanam jagṛhuḥ tasya cira abhyāsena mohitāḥ ūcuḥ tam asurāḥ sarve kruddhāḥ saṃrakta locanāḥ ayam guruḥ hite asmākam gaccha tvam na asi naḥ guruḥ bhārgavaḥ aṅgirasaḥ vā ayam bhavatu eva eṣa naḥ guruḥ bodhitāḥ hi mayā yasmāt na mām bhajata dānavāḥ tasmāt pranaṣṭa saṃjñām vai parābhavan gamiṣyatha vyāhṛtya tān kāvyaḥ jagāma atha yathāgatam kṛtārthaḥ sa tadā hṛṣṭaḥ svam rūpam pratyapadyata buddhvā asurān tadā bhraṣṭān kṛtārthaḥ antaradhīyata tatas pranaṣṭe tasmin te vibhrāntāḥ dānavāḥ tadā pṛṣṭhatas vimukhāḥ ca eva tāḍitāḥ vedhasā vayam dagdhāḥ ca eva upayogāt ca sve sve ca artheṣu māyayā prahlādam agratas kṛtvā kāvyasya anugamam punar tatas kāvyam samāsādya abhitasthuḥ ravāṅmukhāḥ tān āgatān punar dṛṣṭvā kāvyaḥ yājyān uvāca ha mayā api bodhitāḥ kāle yatas mām na abhinandatha svān yājyān bhajamānān ca bhaktān ca eva viśeṣataḥ tvayā pṛṣṭāḥ vayam tena devācāryeṇa mohitāḥ bhaktān arhasi naḥ trātum jñātvā dīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā jñātvā kāvyaḥ yathātattvam kāruṇyena anukampayā na śakyam anyathā kartum dṛṣṭam hi balavattaram saṃjñā pranaṣṭā yā vaḥ adya kāmam tām pratilapsyatha prāptaḥ paryyāya kālaḥ vaḥ iti brahmā abhyabhāṣata yuga ākhyaḥ daśa saṃpūrṇaḥ devān ākramya mūrddhani tāvantam eva kālam vai brahmā rājyam abhāṣata lokānām īśvaraḥ bhāvī pautraḥ tava punar baliḥ yasmāt pravṛttayaḥ ca asya na kāma an abhisandhitāḥ deva rājyam baleḥ bhāvyam iti mām īśvaraḥ abravīt tasmāt adṛśyaḥ bhūtānām kāla ākāṅkṣī sa tiṣṭhati brahmaṇā pratiṣiddhaḥ asmi bhaviṣyam jānatā prabho daivataiḥ saha saṃrabdhān sarvān vaḥ dhārayiṣyataḥ evam uktaḥ tu daiteyāḥ kāvyena akliṣṭa karmmaṇā tatas tābhyām yayuḥ sārddham prahlāda pramukhāḥ tadā avaśyambhāvam artha tvam śrutvā śukrāt ca dānavāḥ sakṛt āśaṃsamānāḥ te jayam kāvyena bhāṣitam daṃśitāḥ sa āyudhāḥ sarve tatas devān samāhvayan atha deva asurān dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme samupasthitān tatas saṃvṛtta sannāhāḥ devāḥ tān samayodhayan daiva āsure tatas tasmin varttamāne śatam samāḥ ṣaṇḍāmārka prabhāvam na suraiḥ vayam tasmāt yajñam samuddiśya kāryyam ca ātma hitam ca yat atha upāmantrayan devāḥ ṣaṇḍāmārkau tu tau ubhau graham tam vā grahīṣyāmaḥ hi anujitya tu dānavān evam tatyajatuḥ tau tu ṣaṇḍāmārkau tadā asurān tatas devāḥ jayam prāptāḥ dānavāḥ ca parābhavam deva asurān parābhāvya ṣaṇḍāmārkau upāgaman kāvya śāpa abhibhūtāḥ ca hi anādhārāḥ ca te punar evam nirudyamāḥ te vai kṛtāḥ śakreṇa dānavāḥ jajñe punar punar viṣṇuḥ yajñe ca śithile prabhuḥ manuṣya vadhyān tān sarvvān brahmā vyāhārayat prabhuḥ dharmmāt nārāyaṇaḥ tasmāt sambhūtaḥ cākṣuṣe antare caturthyām tu yuga ākhyāyām āpanneṣu asureṣu atha dvitīyaḥ narasiṃṅaḥ abhūt rudraḥ sura purassaraḥ dvijaḥ bhūtvā śubhe kāle balim vairocanam purā dadāmi iti eva tam rājā baliḥ vairocanaḥ abravīt sa vāmanaḥ divam kham ca pṛthivīm ca dvijottamāḥ atyaricyata bhūtātmā bhāskaram svena tejasā prakāśayan diśaḥ sarvvāḥ pradiśaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ śuśubhe sa mahā bāhuḥ sarvva lokān prakāśayan āsurīm śriyam āhṛtya trīn lokān ca janārdanaḥ namuciḥ śambaraḥ ca eva prahlādaḥ ca eva viṣṇunā krūrāḥ hatāḥ vinirddhūtāḥ diśaḥ saṃpratipedire mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā sa viśeṣāṇi mādhavaḥ kālam ca sakalam viprān tatra adbhutam adarśayat na kiñcid asti lokeṣu yat avyāptam mahātmanā dṛṣṭvā sammumuhuḥ sarve viṣṇu tejaḥ vimohitāḥ baliḥ silaḥ mahā pāśaiḥ sa bandhuḥ sa suhṛd gaṇaḥ mānuṣeṣu mahā bāhuḥ prādurāsīt janārdanaḥ etāḥ tisraḥ smṛtāḥ tasya divyāḥ sambhūtayaḥ śubhāḥ mānuṣyāḥ sapta yāḥ tasya śāpa jān tān nibodhata naṣṭe dharme caturthaḥ ca mārkaṇḍeya puraḥsaraḥ pañcamaḥ pañcadaśyām tu tretāyām sambabhūva ha jāmadagnyaḥ tathā ṣaṣṭaḥ viśvāmitra puraḥsaraḥ caturviṃśe yuge rāmaḥ vasiṣṭena purodhasā saptamaḥ rāva ṇasya arthe jajñe daśaratha ātmajaḥ aṣṭamaḥ dvāpare viṣṇuḥ aṣṭāviṃśe parāśarāt vedavyāsaḥ tatas jajñe jātūkarṇa puraḥsaraḥ tathā eva navamaḥ viṣṇuḥ adityāḥ kaśyapa ātmajaḥ na pramātum mahā bāhuḥ śakyaḥ asau madhusūdanaḥ aṣṭāviṃśa time tadvat dvāparasya aṃśa saṅkṣaye naṣṭe dharme tadā jajñe viṣṇuḥ vṛṣṇi kule prabhuḥ karttum dharma vyavasthānam asurāṇām praṇāśanam mohayan sarva bhūtāni yoga ātmā yoga māyayā praviṣṭaḥ mānuṣīm yonim pracchannaḥ carate mahīm vihāra artham manuṣyeṣu sāndīpani puraḥsaram yatra kaṃsañca śālvañca dvividañca mahā asuram ariṣṭam vṛṣabham ca eva pūtanām keśinam hayam nāgam kuvalayāpīḍam malla rāja gṛha adhipam daityān mānuṣa deha sthān sūdayāmāsa vīryavān chinnam bāhu sahasrañca bāṇasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ narakaḥ ca hataḥ saṅkhaye yavanaḥ ca mahā balaḥ hṛtāni ca mahīpānām sarva ratnāni tejasā durācārāḥ śca nihatāḥ pārthivāḥ ye rasātale ete loka hita arthāya prādurbhāvāḥ mahātmanaḥ asmin eva yuge kṣīṇe sandhyā śliṣṭe bhaviṣyati kalkiḥ viṣṇuyaśāḥ nāma pārāśaryaḥ pratāpavān daśamaḥ bhāvya sambhūtaḥ yājñavalkya puraḥsaraḥ pragṛhīta āyudhauḥ vipraiḥ vṛtaḥ śata sahasraśas īdīcyān madhyadeśān ca tathā vindhya aparāntikān tathā eva dākṣiṇātyān ca dravijān siṃhalaiḥ saha gāndhārān pāradān ca eva pahlavān yavanān śakān lampākān andhakān rudrān kirātān ca eva sa prabhuḥ adṛśyaḥ sarva bhūtānām pṛthivīm vicariṣyati mānavaḥ sa tu saṃjajñe devasya aṃśena dhīmataḥ pūrva janmani viṣṇuḥ yaḥ pramitiḥ nāma vīryavān iti etāḥ tasya devasya daśa sambhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ tam tam kālam ca kāryam ca tat tat uddiśya kāraṇam aṃśena triṣu lokeṣu tāḥ tāḥ yonīḥ prapatsyate pañcaviṃśa utthite kalpe pañcaviṃśati vai samāḥ vinighnan sarvva bhūtāni mānuṣān eva sarvvaśas kṛtvā bīja avaśeṣām tu mahīm krūreṇa karmmaṇā saṃśātayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśas tān adhārmmikān akasmāt kupita anyonyam bhaviṣyanti ca mohitāḥ kṣapayitvā tu tān sarvān bāvinā arthena coditān gaṅgā yamunayoḥ madhye niṣṭām prāpsyati sa anugaḥ nṛpeṣu atha vinaṣṭeṣu tadā tu apragrahāḥ prajāḥ rakṣaṇe vinivṛtte tu hatvā ca anyonyam āhave purāṇi hitvā grāmān ca tulyāḥ tāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ pranaṣṭa śruti dharmāḥ ca naṣṭa dharma āśramāḥ tathā sarit parvata sevinyaḥ patra mūla phala aśanāḥ cīra pattra ajina dharāḥ saṅkaram ghoram āsthitāḥ alpa āyuṣaḥ naṣṭa vārttāḥ bahu ābādhāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ evam kaṣṭam anuprāptāḥ kali sandhi aṃśake tadā prajāḥ kṣayam prayāsyanti sārddham kali yugena tu kṣīṇe kali yuge tasmin pravṛtte ca kṛte punar prapatsyante yathānyāyam svabhāvāt eva na anyatā iti etat kīrtitam sarvam deva asura viceṣṭitam yadu vaṃśa prasaṅgena mahat vaḥ vaiṣṇavam yaśaḥ anyaḥ tu avīkṣitaḥ rājā maruttaḥ kathitaḥ purā evam yayā ādi śāpena jarāyāḥ saṃkrameṇa tu turvasoḥ pauravam vaṃśam praviveśa purā kila duṣkṛtasya tu dāyādaḥ śarūthaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ śarūthāt tu janāpīḍaḥ catvāraḥ tasya ca ātmajāḥ teṣām janapadāḥ kulyāḥ pāṇḍyāḥ colāḥ sa keralāḥ yuddham su mahat āsīt tu māsān pari caturdaśa aruddhasya tu dāyādaḥ gāndhāraḥ nāma pārthivaḥ khyāyate yasya nāmnā tu gāndhāra viṣayaḥ mahān gāndhāra deśa jāḥ ca api turagāḥ vājinām varāḥ pracetasaḥ putra śatam rājānaḥ sarve eva te mleccha rāṣṭra adhipāḥ sarve hi udīcīm diśam āśritāḥ anoḥ putrāḥ mahātmānaḥ trayaḥ parama dhārmmikāḥ sabhānarasya putraḥ tu vidvān kālānalaḥ nṛpaḥ kāla analasya dharmma ātmā sṛñjayaḥ nāma dhārmikaḥ sṛñjayasya abhavat putraḥ vīraḥ rājā purañjayaḥ āsīt indra samaḥ rājā pratiṣṭita yaśāḥ divi mahāmanāḥ sutaḥ tasya mahā śālasya dhārmikaḥ uśīnaram ca dharma jñam titikṣum ca eva dhārmikam uśīnarasya patnyaḥ tu pañca rājarṣi vaṃśa jāḥ mṛgā kṛmī navā darvā pañcamī ca dṛṣadvatī uśīnarasya putrāḥ tu pañca tāsu kula udvahāḥ tapasā te su mahatā jāta vṛddhāḥ ca dhārmikāḥ mṛgāyāḥ tu mṛgaḥ putraḥ navāyāḥ navaḥ eva tu kṛmyāḥ kṛmiḥ tu darvāyāḥ suvrataḥ nāma dhārmikaḥ dṛṣadvatī sutaḥ ca api śiviḥ auśīnaraḥ dvijāḥ śiveḥ śivapuram khyātam mṛgasya tu navasya kṛmeḥ tu kṛmilā purī suvratasya tathā vṛṣṭā śivi putrān nibodhata śiveḥ tu śivayaḥ putrāḥ catvāraḥ loka sammatāḥ teṣām janapadāḥ sphītāḥ kekayāḥ mādrakāḥ tathā vṛṣa darbhāḥ sūci darbhāḥ titikṣoḥ śrṛṇuta prajāḥ taitikṣuḥ abhavat rājā pūrvasyān diśi viśrutaḥ hemasya sutapāḥ jajñe sutaḥ sutayaśāḥ balī jātaḥ manuṣya yonyām vai kṣīṇe vaṃśe prajepsayā mahā yogī sa tu baliḥ baddhaḥ yaḥ sa mahā manāḥ putrān utpādayāmāsa cāturvarṇya karān bhuvi aṅgam sa janayāmāsa vaṅgam suhlam tathā eva ca puṇḍram kaliṅgam ca tathā bāleyam kṣatram ucyate bāleyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva tasya vaṃśa karāḥ prabhoḥ baleḥ tu brahmaṇā dattāḥ varāḥ prītena dhīmate mahāyogi tvam āyuḥ ca kalpa āyuḥ parimāṇakam iti uktaḥ vibhunā rājā baliḥ śāntim parām yayau kālena mahatā vidvān svam vai sthānam upāgataḥ teṣām janapadāḥ sphītāḥ vaṅga aṅga suhlakāḥ tathā puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca tathā teṣām vaṃśam tasya te tanayāḥ sarve kṣetrajāḥ muni sambhavāḥ sambhūtāḥ dīrghatamasaḥ sudeṇṇāyām mahā ojasaḥ katham baleḥ sutāḥ pañca janitāḥ kṣetrajāḥ prabho ṛṣiṇā dīrghatamasā etat naḥ brūhi pṛcchatām aśijaḥ nāma vikhyātaḥ āsīt hi imā nṛṣiḥ purā bhāryā vai samatā nāma babhūva asya mahātmanaḥ aśijasya kanīyān tu purodhāḥ yaḥ divaukasām antarvatnī asmi te bhrātuḥ jyeṣṭhasya aṣṭamitā iti brahmacā abhyasya ṣaṣ aṅgam vedam udgiran kāma ātmānam mahātmā ca na ātmānam saḥ abhyadhārayat sambabhūva eva dharma ātmā tayā sārddham bṛhaspatiḥ amogha retāḥ tvañca api pūrvam ca aham iha āgataḥ śaśāpa tam tadā kruddhaḥ evam uktaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ sutam bhrātuḥ garbha stham bhagavān ṛṣiḥ yasmāt tvam īdṛśe kāle sarva bhūta īpsite sati tatas dīrghatamāḥ nāma śāpāt ṛṣiḥ ajāyata atha āśijaḥ bṛhat kīrttiḥ bṛhaspatiḥ iva ojasā ūrddhvaretāḥ tatas ca api nyavasat bhrātuḥ āśrame tasya bhrātā pitṛvyaḥ tu cakāra bhavanam tadā tasmin hi tatra vasati yadṛcchā abhyāgataḥ vṛṣaḥ darśa artham āhṛtān darbhān cacāra surabhī vṛtaḥ jagrāha tam dīrghatamāḥ visphurantam ca śrṛṅgayoḥ tatas abravīt vṛṣaḥ tam vai muñca mām balinām vara muñca mām balinām śraṣṭha prītaḥ te aham varam vṛṇu tena tvā aham na mokṣyāmi parasva aham catuṣpadam tatas tam dīrghatamasam sa vṛṣaḥ pratyuvāca ha na asmākam vidyate tāta pātakam steyam eva vā bhakṣya abhakṣyam na jānīmaḥ peya apeyam ca sarvaśas na pāpmānaḥ vayam vipra dharmaḥ hi eṣām gavām smṛtaḥ gavām nāma sa vai śrutvā saṃbhrāntaḥ tu anumucya tam bhaktyā ca ānuśravikayā goṣu tam vai manasā eva tat ādatte tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ viceṣṭamānām rudatīm daivāt sa mūḍha cetanaḥ avalepan tu tam matvā śaradvān tasya na akṣamat go dharmam vai balam kṛtvā snuṣām sa samamanyata tam dṛṣṭvā śaradvān pratyacintayat bhaviṣyam artham jñātvā ca mahātmā ca na mṛtyu tām gamya agamyam na jīnīṣe go dharmāt prārthayat snuṣām uhyamānaḥ samudraḥ tu sapta aham srotasā tadā apaśyat majjamānam tu srotasā abhyāśam āgatam tam gṛhītvā sa dharma ātmā baliḥ vairocanaḥ tadā sa ca tasmāt varam vavre putra artham dānava ṛṣabhaḥ santāna artham mahābhāga bhāryayā mama mānadaḥ sudeṣṇām nāma bāryām vai rājā asmai prāhiṇot tadā andham vṛddham ca tam dṛṣṭvā na sā devī jagāma ha svān ca dhātreyakīm tasmai bhūṣayitvā vyasarjayat kakṣīva cakṣuṣau tasyām śūdra yonyām ṛṣiḥ vaśī tau tu dṛṣṭvā rājā baliḥ tadā anadham bṛddham ca mām matvā sudeṣṇā mahiṣī tava prāhiṇot avamānāya śūdrām dhātreyakīm mama tatas prasādayāmāsa punar tam ṛṣi sattamam baliḥ bhāryām sudeṣṇām ca bhartsayāmāsa vai prabhuḥ punar ca enām alaṃkṛtya ṛṣaye pratyapādayat tām sa dīrghatamāḥ devīm abravīt yadi mām śubhe dadhnā lavaṇa miśreṇa sva byaktam nagnakam tathā tasya sā tat vacaḥ devī sarvam kṛtavatī tathā tām uvāca tatas sa ṛṣiḥ yat te parihṛtam śubhe vinā apānam kumāram tvam janayiṣyasi pūrvajam tatas tam dīrghatamasam sā devī pratyuvāca ha na arhasi tvam mahābhāga putram dātum mama īdṛśam tava aparādhaḥ devi eṣa na anyathā bhavitā anu vai devī dānīm ca te putram aham dāsyāmi suvrate tasya apānam vinā ca eva yogyā bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati tām sa dīrghatamāḥ ca eva kukṣau spṛṣṭvā idam abravavīt prāśitam dadhi yat te adya mama aṅgāt vai śuci smite tena te pūritaḥ garbhaḥ paurṇamāsyām iva udadhiḥ bhaviṣyanti kumārāḥ te pañca deva suta upamāḥ tejasvinaḥ parākrāntāḥ yajvānaḥ dhārmikāḥ tathā tatas uṅgaḥ tu sudeṣṇāyāḥ jyeṣṭha putraḥ vyajāyata vaṃśa bhājaḥ tu pañca ete baleḥ kṣetre abhavan tadā iti ete dīrghatamasā baleḥ dattāḥ sutāḥ purā prajāḥ tu apahatāḥ tasya brahmaṇā kāraṇam prati apatyā mātya dāreṣu sveṣu mā bhūt mahātmanaḥ tatas manuṣya yonyām vai janayāmāsa sa prajāḥ jarā mṛtyu bhayañca eva āghrāya praṇudāmi te hi āghrāta mātraḥ saḥ apaśyata sadyas tamasi nāśite āyuṣmān ca yuvā ca eva cakṣuṣmān ca tatas abhavat kakṣīvān tu tatas gatvā saha pitrā giri prajām tatas kālena mahatā tamasā bhāvitaḥ vidhūya manujaḥ doṣān brahmaṇyam prāptavān prabhuḥ sat putreṇa tvayā tāta kṛtārthaḥ asmi yaśasvinā yukta ātmā hi tatas saḥ atha prāptavān brahmaṇā kṣayam brahmaṇyam prāpya kakṣīvān sahasram asṛjat sutān kṛṣṇa aṅgāḥ gautamāḥ te vai smṛtāḥ kakṣīvataḥ sutāḥ samāgamaḥ samākhyātaḥ santānam ca ubhayoḥ tayoḥ baliḥ tān abiṣicya iha pañca putrān akalmaṣān kṛtārthaḥ saḥ api yoga ātmā yogam āśritya ca prabhuḥ adṛśyaḥ sarva bhūtānām kāla ākāṅkṣī carati uta tatra aṅgasya tu rājarṣe rājā āsīt dadhivāhanaḥ sa aparādha sudeṣṇāyāḥ anapānaḥ abhava nṛpaḥ anapānasya putraḥ tu rājā divirathaḥ smṛtaḥ vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca pūroḥ tu śrṛṇuta prajāḥ raudrāśvasya ghṛtācyām vai daśa apsarasi sūnavaḥ rudrā śūdrā ca madrā ca śubhā jāmalajā tathā talā khalā ca saptā etāḥ yā ca gopajalā smṛtā tathā tāmrarasā ca eva ratnakūṭī ca tādṛśī yasmāt mām īdṛśe kāle sarva bhūta īpsite sati bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ suhotraḥ nāma dhārmikaḥ tapasaḥ ante su mahataḥ rājñaḥ vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ vibhrājasya tu dāyādaḥ tu aṇuhaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ imam ca udāharanti atra ślokam prati mahābhiṣam subhadrāyām rathī pārthāt abhimanyuḥ ajāyata kṣemakam prāpya rājānam saṃsthām prāpsyati vai kalau ete aikṣvākavāḥ proktāḥ bhavitāraḥ kalau yuge śūrāḥ ca kṛtavidyāḥ ca satya sandhāḥ jita indriyāḥ atra anuvaṃśa ślokaḥ ayam bhaviṣya jñaiḥ udāhṛtaḥ ikṣvākūṇām ayam vaṃśaḥ sumitrā antaḥ bhaviṣyati sumitram prāpya rājānam saṃsthām prāpsyati vai kalau iti etat mānavam kṣetramailam ca samudāhṛtam atas ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi māgadheyān bṛhadrathān jarāsandhasya ye vaṃśe sahadeva anvaye nṛpāḥ atītāḥ varttamānāḥ ca bhaviṣyāḥ ca tathā punar pañcāśatam tathā aṣṭau ca samāḥ rājyam akārayat śrutaśravāḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi samāḥ tasya sutaḥ abhavat ayuta āyūḥ tu ṣaḍviṃśam rājyam varṣāṇi akārayat samāḥ śatam nirāmitraḥ mahīm bhuktvā divaṅgataḥ pañcāśatam samāḥ ṣaḍ ca sukṛttaḥ prāptavān mahīm trayoviṃśam bṛhatkarmā rājyam varṣāṇi akārayat senājit sāmpratam ca api etām vai bhujyate samāḥ śrutañjayaḥ tu varṣāṇi catvāriṃśat bhaviṣyati pañcatriṃśat tu varṣāṇi mahīm pālayitā nṛpaḥ aṣṭa pañcā śatam ca abdān rājye sthāsyati vai śuciḥ aṣṭāviṃśat samāḥ pūrṇāḥ kṣemaḥ rājā bhaviṣyati bhuvataḥ tu catuḥṣaṣṭī rājyam prāpsyati vīryyavān pañca varṣāṇi pūrṇāni dharmanetraḥ bhaviṣyati bhokṣyate nṛpatiḥ ca eva hi aṣṭapañcāśatam samāḥ aṣṭātriṃśat samāḥ rājyam suvratasya bhaviṣyati catvāriṃśat daśa aṣṭau ca dṛḍhasenaḥ bhaviṣyati trayastriṃśat tu varṣāṇi sumatiḥ prāpsyate tatas catvāriṃśat samāḥ rājā sunetraḥ bhokṣyate tatas satyajit pṛthivī rājyam tri aśītim bhokṣyate samāḥ prāpya imām vīrajit ca api pañcatriṃśat bhaviṣyati arīn jayaḥ tu varṣāṇi pañcāśat prāpsyate mahīm dvātriṃśat ca nṛpāḥ hi ete bhavitāraḥ bṛhat rathāḥ pūrṇam varṣa sahasram vai teṣām rājyam bhaviṣyati bṛhadratheṣu atīteṣu vītahotreṣu munikaḥ svāminam hatvā putram samabhiṣekṣyati miṣatām kṣatriyāṇām hi pradyotaḥ munikaḥ balāt trayoviṃśat samāḥ rājā bhavitā sa nara uttamaḥ caturviṃśat samāḥ rājā pālakaḥ bhavitā tatas viśākha yūpaḥ bhavitā nṛpaḥ pañcāśatīm samāḥ aṣṭātriṃśat śatam bhāvyāḥ prādyotāḥ pañca te sutāḥ hatvā teṣām yaśaḥ kṛtsnam śiśunākaḥ bhaviṣyati vārāṇasyām sutaḥ tasya saṃprāpsyati girivrajam śiśunākasya varṣāṇi catvāriṃśat bhaviṣyati śakavarṇaḥ sutaḥ tasya ṣaṭtriṃśat ca bhaviṣyati tatas tu viṃśatim rājā kṣemavarmā bhaviṣyati ajātaśatrūḥ bhavitā pañcaviṃśat samāḥ nṛpaḥ catvāriṃśat samāḥ rājyam kṣatraujāḥ prāpsyate tatas aṣṭāviṃśat samāḥ rājā vivisāraḥ bhaviṣyati pañcaviṃśat samāḥ rājā darśakaḥ tu bhaviṣyati udāyī bhavitā tasmāt trayastriṃśat samāḥ nṛpaḥ sa vai puravaram rājā pṛthivyām kusumāhvayam gaṅgāyāḥ dakṣiṇe kūle caturthe abde kariṣyati dvācatvāriṃśat samāḥ bhāvyaḥ rājā vai nandivarddhanaḥ catvāriṃśat trayam ca eva mahā nandī bhaviṣyati aikṣvākavāḥ caturviṃśat pāñcālāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ kālakāḥ tu caturvviṃśat caturvviṃśatī tu haihayāḥ dvātriṃśat vai kaliṅgāḥ tu pañcaviṃśat tathā śakāḥ kuravaḥ ca api ṣaḍviṃśat aṣṭāviṃśati maithilāḥ śūrasenāḥ trayoviṃśat vītihotrāḥ ca viṃśatiḥ tulya kālam bhaviṣyanti sarve eva mahīkṣitaḥ mahānandi sutaḥ ca api śūdrāyām kāla saṃvṛtaḥ tatas prabhṛti rājānaḥ bhaviṣyāḥ śūdra yonayaḥ aṣṭau viṃśati varṣāṇi pṛthivīm pālayiṣyati sahasrāḥ tad sutāḥ hi aṣṭau samāḥ dvādaśa te nṛpāḥ mahāpadmasya paryāye bhaviṣyanti nṛpāḥ kramāt uddhariṣyati tān sarvān kauṭilyaḥ vai dvis aṣṭabhiḥ bhuktvā mahīm varṣa śatam nanda induḥ sa bhaviṣyati candraguptam nṛpam rājye kauṭilyaḥ sthāpayiṣyati caturviṃśat samāḥ rājā candraguptaḥ bhaviṣyati bhavitā bhadra sāraḥ tu pañcaviṃśat samāḥ nṛpaḥ tasya putraḥ kunālaḥ tu varṣāṇi aṣṭau bhaviṣyati kunāla sūnuḥ aṣṭau ca bhoktā vai bandhu pālitaḥ bandhu pālita dāyādaḥ daśa māni indra pālitaḥ bhavitā sapta varṣāṇi devavarmmā narādhipaḥ rājā śatadharaḥ ca aṣṭau tasya putraḥ bhaviṣyati bṛhadaśvaḥ ca varṣāṇi sapta vai bhavitā nṛpaḥ kārayiṣyati vai rājyam samāḥ ṣaṣṭim sadā eva tu puṣpamitra sutāḥ ca aṣṭau bhaviṣyanti samāḥ nṛpāḥ bhavitā ca api tad jyeṣṭhaḥ sapta varṣāṇi vai tatas vasumitraḥ sutaḥ bhāvyaḥ daśa varṣāṇi pārthivaḥ rājā ghoṣa sutaḥ ca api varṣāṇi bhavitā trayaḥ dvātriṃśat bhavitā ca api samāḥ bhāgavataḥ nṛpaḥ bhaviṣyati sutaḥ tasya kṣema bhūmiḥ samāḥ daśa daśā ete tuṅga rājānaḥ bhokṣyanti imām vasundharam śatam pūrṇam daśa dve ca tebhyaḥ kim vā gamiṣyati devabhūmiḥ tatas anyaḥ ca śrṛṅgeṣu bhavitā nṛpaḥ bhaviṣyati samāḥ rājā nava kaṇṭāyanaḥ tu saḥ bhavitā dvādaśa samāḥ tasmāt nārāyaṇaḥ nṛpaḥ suśarmmā tad sutaḥ ca api bhaviṣyati samāḥ daśa kaṇṭāyanam athā uddhṛtya suśarmmāṇam prasahya tam sindhukaḥ hi andhra jātīyaḥ prāpsyati imām vasundharām trayoviṃśat samāḥ rājā sindhukaḥ bhavitā tu atha pañcāśatam samāḥ ṣaḍ ca sātakarṇiḥ bhaviṣyati caturvviṃśat tu varṣāṇi ṣaḍ samāḥ vai bhaviṣyati tatas saṃvatsaram pūrṇam hālaḥ rājā bhaviṣyati bhāvyaḥ putrikaṣeṇaḥ tu samāḥ saḥ api ekaviṃśatim sātakarṇiḥ varṣam ekam bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ aṣṭāviṃśat tu varṣāṇi śivasvāmī bhaviṣyati rājā ca gautamīputraḥ ekaviṃśat samāḥ nṛṣu ekonaviṃśatim rājā yajñaśrīḥ sātakarṇī atha ṣaṣ eva bhavitā tasmāt vijayaḥ tu samāḥ nṛpaḥ daṇḍaśrīḥ sātakarṇī ca tasya putraḥ samāḥ trayaḥ iti ete vai nṛpāḥ triṃśat andhrāḥ bhokṣyanti ye mahīm samāḥ śatāni catvāri pañca ṣaḍ vai tathā eva ca andhrāṇām saṃsthitāḥ pañca teṣām vaṃśāḥ samāḥ punar sapta eva tu bhaviṣyanti daśa ābhīrāḥ tatas nṛpāḥ sapta gardabhinaḥ ca api tatas atha daśa vai śakāḥ yavana aṣṭau bhaviṣyanti tuṣārāḥ tu caturdaśa trayodaśa maruṇḍāḥ ca maunāḥ hi aṣṭādaśa eva tu andhrāḥ bhokṣyanti vasudhām śate dve ca śatam ca vai śatāni trīṇi aśītiṃca bhokṣyanti vasudhām śakāḥ aśītiṃ ca eva varṣāṇi bhoktāraḥ yavanāḥ mahīm pañca varṣa śatāni iha tuṣārāṇām mahī smṛtā maruṇḍāḥ vṛṣalaiḥ sārddham bhāvyāḥ anyāḥ mleccha jātayaḥ śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyanti mlecchāḥ ekādaśa eva tu samāḥ ṣaṇṇavatim trātvā pṛthivīm ca sameṣyati śeṣasya nāga rājasya putraḥ svarapurañjayaḥ bhogī bhaviṣyate rājā nṛpaḥ nāga kula udvahaḥ sadācandraḥ tu candrāṃśaḥ dvitīyaḥ nakhavān tathā dhanadharmā tatas ca api caturthaḥ viṃśa jaḥ smṛtaḥ tasya bhrātā yavīyān tu nāmnā nandiyaśāḥ kila dohitraḥ śiśukaḥ nāma purikāyām nṛpaḥ abhavat vindhyaśakti sutaḥ ca api pravīraḥ nāma vīryavān bhokṣyanti ca samāḥ ṣaṣṭim purīm vai yakṣyanti vājapeyaiḥ ca samāpta vara dakṣiṇaiḥ vindhyakānām kule atīte nṛpāḥ vai bāhlikāḥ strayaḥ śakyamāḥ nāma vai rājā māhiṣīnām mahīpatiḥ puṣpamitrāḥ bhaviṣyanti paṭṭamitrāḥ trayodaśa mekalāyām nṛpāḥ sapta bhaviṣyanti ca sattamāḥ rājānaḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā balāḥ naiṣadhāḥ pārthivāḥ sarvve bhaviṣyantyām anu kṣayāt nala vaṃśa prasūtāḥ te vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ māgadhānām mahā vīryaḥ viśvasphāniḥ bhaviṣyati utsādya pārthivān sarvān saḥ anyān varṇān kariṣyati kaivarttān pañcakān ca eva pulindān brāhmaṇān tathā sthāpayiṣyanti rājānaḥ nānā deśeṣu tejasā viśvasphāniḥ narapatiḥ klībā kṛtiḥ iva ucyate nava nākāḥ tu bhokṣyanti purīm campāvatīm nṛpāḥ mathurām ca purīm ramyām nāgāḥ bhokṣyanti sapta vai anugaṅgam prayāgam ca sāketam magadhān tathā etān janapadān sarvvān bhokṣyante gupta vaṃśa jāḥ niṣadhān yadukān ca eva tān kālatopakān etān janapadān sarvvān bhokṣyanti maṇidhānya jāḥ kośalān ca andhrapauṇḍrān ca tāmraliptān sa sāgarān campām ca eva purīm ramyām bhokṣyanti deva rakṣitām kāliṅgāḥ mahiṣāḥ ca eva mahendra nilayāḥ ca ye etān janapadān sarvān pālayiṣyati vai guhaḥ strī rāṣṭram bhakṣyakān ca eva bhokṣyate kanakāhvayaḥ alpa prasādāḥ hi anṛtāḥ mahā krodhāḥ hi adhārmikāḥ na eva mūrddhābhiṣiktāḥ te bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ yuga doṣa durācārāḥ bhaviṣyanti nṛpāḥ tu te bhaviṣyanti iha paryāye kālena pṛthivīkṣitaḥ taiḥ vimiśrāḥ janapadāḥ mleccha ācārāḥ ca sarvaśas lubdha anṛta ratāḥ ca eva bhavitāraḥ tadā nṛpāḥ teṣām vyatīte paryāye bahu strīke yuge tadā lavāt lavam bhraśyamānāḥ āyū rūpa bala śrutaiḥ tathā gatāḥ tu vai kāṣṭām prajāsu jagatī īśvarāḥ rājānaḥ sampraṇaśyanti kālena upahatāḥ tadā adhārmikāḥ ca te atyartham pāṣaṇḍāḥ ca eva sarvaśas pranaṣṭe nṛpa śabde ca sandhyā āśliṣṭe kalau yuge kiṃñcid śiṣṭāḥ prajāḥ tāḥ vai dharmme naṣṭe aparigrahāḥ anāvṛṣṭi hatāḥ ca eva paraspara vadhena ca anāthāḥ hi paritrastāḥ vārttām utsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ tyaktvā purāṇi grāmān ca bhaviṣyanti vanaukasaḥ evam nṛpeṣu naṣṭeṣu prajāḥ tyaktvā gṛhāṇi tu naṣṭe snehe durāpannāḥ bhraṣṭa snehāḥ suhṛd janāḥ varṇa āśrama paribhraṣṭāḥ saṅkaram ghoram āsthitāḥ saritaḥ sāgara anūpān sevante parvatāni ca aṅgān kaliṅgān vaṅgān ca kāśmīrān kāśi kośalān ṛṣikānta giri droṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ kṛtsnam himavataḥ pṛṣṭham kūlam ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ mṛgaiḥ mīnaiḥ vihaṅgaiḥ ca śvāpadaiḥ takṣubhiḥ tathā madhu śāka phalaiḥ mūlaiḥ varttayiṣyanti mānavāḥ cīram parṇam ca vividham valkalāni ajināni ca bīja annāni tathā kāṣṭha śaṅkubhiḥ aja eḍakam khara uṣṭram ca pālayiṣyanti yatnataḥ nadīḥ vatsyanti toya arthe kūlam āśritya mānavāḥ bahu manyāḥ prajā hīnāḥ śauca ācāra vivarjitāḥ hīnāt hīnān tathā dharmmān prajāḥ samanuvarttate āyuḥ tadā trayoviṃśam na kaścid ativarttate durbalāḥ viṣaya glānāḥ jarayā saṃpariplutāḥ patra mūla phala āhārāḥ cīra kṛṣṇa ajina ambarāḥ etad kālam anuprāptāḥ prajāḥ kali yuga antake niḥśeṣāḥ tu bhaviṣyanti sārddham kali yugena tu sa sandhyāṃśe tu niḥśeṣe kṛtam vai pratipatsyate yadā candraḥ ca sūryaḥ ca tathā tiṣya bṛhaspatī eṣa vaṃśa kramaḥ kṛtsnam kīrtitaḥ vaḥ yathākramam atītāḥ varttamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ ca ye mahādeva abhiṣekāt tu janma yāvat parikṣitaḥ pramāṇam vai tathā ca uktam mahāpadma antaram ca yat antaram tat śatāni aṣṭau ṣaṭtriṃśat ca samāḥ smṛtāḥ etad kāla antaram bhāvyāḥ andhra antāḥ ye prakīrttitāḥ bhaviṣyaiḥ tatra saṅkhyātāḥ purāṇa jñaiḥ śruta ṛṣibhiḥ saptarṣayaḥ tadā prāhuḥ pratīpe rājñi vai śatam saptaviṃśaiḥ śataiḥ bhāvyāḥ andhrāṇām te tvayā punar saptarṣayaḥ tu tiṣṭhanti paryāyeṇa śatam śatam saptarṣīṇām yugam hi etat divyayā saṅkhyayā smṛtam saptarṣīṇām tu ye pūrvāḥ dṛśyante uttarā diśi tena saptarṣayaḥ yuktāḥ jñeyāḥ vyomni śatam samāḥ nakṣatrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ca yogasya etat nidarśanam saptarṣayaḥ maghā yuktāḥ kāle pārikṣite śatam imāḥ tadā tu prakṛtiḥ vyāpatsyanti prajāḥ bhṛśam anṛta upahatāḥ sarvāḥ dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ śrauta smārtte praśithile dharme varṇa āśrame tadā śaṅkaram durbala ātmānaḥ pratipatsyanti mohitāḥ saṃsaktāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāḥ sārddham dvijātibhiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śūdra yaṣṭāraḥ śūdrāḥ vai mantra yonayaḥ lavam lavam bhrasyamānāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ krameṇa tu kṣayam eva gamiṣyanti kṣīṇa śeṣāḥ yuga kṣaye yasmin kṛṣṇaḥ divam yātaḥ tasmin eva tadā dine sahasrāṇām śatāni iha trīṇi mānuṣa saṅkhyayā ṣaṣṭim ca eva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām ucyate kaliḥ niḥśeṣe ca tadā tasmin kṛtam vai pratipatsyate ailaḥ ikṣvāku vaṃśaḥ ca saha bhedaiḥ prakīrttitau ikṣvākoḥ tu smṛtaḥ kṣatraḥ sumitrā antam vivasvataḥ ailam kṣatram kṣemakāntam soma vaṃśa vidaḥ viduḥ ete vivasvataḥ putrāḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrtti varddhanāḥ atītāḥ varttamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ ca ye brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva anvaye smṛtāḥ yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśas bahu tvāt nāmadheyānām parisaṃkhyā kule kule eva āyāntu yuga ākhyāyām yatas kṣatram prapatsyate devāpiḥ pauravaḥ rājā ikṣvākoḥ ca eva yaḥ mataḥ mahā yoga bala upetaḥ kalāpa grāmam āsthitaḥ na ca viṃśe yuge soma vaṃśasya ādiḥ bhaviṣyati evam sarvatra vijñeyam santāna arthe tu lakṣaṇam gotrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām ca bhaviṣyete pravarttakau dvāpara aṃśe na tiṣṭhanti kṣatriyāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saha evam eva tu sarveṣu tiṣṭhanti iha antareṣu vai saptarṣayaḥ nṛpaiḥ sārddham santāna artham yuge yuge manvantarāṇām saptānām santānāḥ ca śrutāḥ ca te yathā pravṛttiḥ teṣām vai pravṛttānām tathā kṣayaḥ saptarṣayaḥ viduḥ teṣām dīrgha āyuḥ tvā akṣayantu te utpadyamānāḥ tretāyām kṣīyamāṇe kalau punar anuyānti yuga ākhyām tu yāvat manvantara kṣayaḥ jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśeṣite kṛte vaṃśa kulāḥ sarvāḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vasudhādhipaiḥ dvi vaṃśa karaṇāḥ ca eva kīrttayiṣye nibodhata rājānaḥ śreṇi baddhāḥ tu tathā anye kṣatriyāḥ nṛpāḥ aila vaṃśasya ye khyātāḥ tathā eva aikṣvākavāḥ nṛpāḥ teṣām ekaśatam pūrṇam kulānām abhiṣekinām tāvat eva tu bhojānām vistāraḥ dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ bhajate triṃśakam kṣatram caturdhā tat yathādiśam teṣu atītāḥ samānāḥ ye bruvataḥ tān nibodhata śatam vai prativindhyānām śatam nāgāḥ śatam hayāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrāḥ ca ekaśatam aśītiḥ janamejayāḥ śatam ca brahmadattānām śīriṇām vīriṇām śatam tatas śatam purā umānām śveta kāśa kuśa ādayaḥ tatas apare sahasram vai ye atītāḥ śata bindavaḥ ījire ca aśvamedhaiḥ te sarve niyuta dakṣiṇaiḥ evam rājarṣayaḥ atītāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣām nibodhata utpannāḥ loke santatayaḥ smṛtāḥ aṣṭāviṃśat yuga ākhyāḥ tu gatāḥ vaivasvate antare etāḥ rājarṣibhiḥ sārddham śiṣṭāḥ yāḥ tāḥ nibodhata catvāriṃśat ca ye ca eva bhaviṣyāḥ saha rājabhiḥ yuga ākhyānām viśiṣṭāḥ tu tatas vaivasvata kṣaye etat vaḥ kathitam sarvvam samāsa vyāsa yogataḥ ete yayāti putrāṇām pañcaviṃśāḥ viśām hitāḥ kīrttitāḥ ca amitāḥ ye me lokān vai dhārayanti uta āyuḥ kīrttim dhanam putrān svargam ca ānantyam aśnute iti eṣa vaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kathitaḥ dvijāḥ śrutvā pādam krāntam sūtena dhīmatā tatas caturtham papracchuḥ pādam vai ṛṣi sattamāḥ pādaḥ krāntaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ayam anuṣaṅgeṇa yaḥ tvayā caturtham vistarāt pādam saṃhāram parikīrttaya manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi pūrvāṇi eva aparaiḥ saha saptarṣīṇām atha eteṣām sāmpratasya antare manoḥ pādam tu imam sa saṃhāram caturtham muni sattamāḥ vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca nisargam śrṛṇuta dvijāḥ manvantarāṇām saṃkṣepam bhaviṣyaiḥ saha saptabhiḥ manvantarāṇi saṃkṣepāt śṛṇuta anāgatāni me anāgatāḥ ca sapta eva smṛtāḥ tu iha mahā ṛṣayaḥ kauśikaḥ gātavaḥ ca eva jāmadagnyaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ dvaipāyanaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tathā ātreyaḥ dīptimān ca eva ṛṣyaśrṛṅgaḥ tu kāśyapaḥ bhāradvājaḥ tathā drauṇiḥ aśvatthāmā mahā yaśāḥ ete sapta mahātmānaḥ bhaviṣyāḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ sutapāḥ ca amitābhāḥ ca sukhāḥ ca eva gaṇāḥ trayaḥ teṣām gaṇāḥ tu devānām ekaikaḥ viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ nāmataḥ tu pravakṣyāmi nibodhadhvam samāhitāḥ prabhāsaḥ bhāsakṛt dharmmaḥ tejoraśmi ṛtuḥ virāj arciṣmān dyotanaḥ bhānuḥ yaśa kīrttiḥ budhaḥ dhṛtiḥ viṃśatiḥ sutapāḥ hi ete nāmabhiḥ parikīrtitāḥ sumatiḥ pramatiḥ dīptiḥ samākhyātaḥ mahaḥ mahān dehaḥ muniḥ nayaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ samaḥ satyaḥ ca viśrutaḥ iti ete hi amita ābhāḥ tu viṃśatiḥ parikīrttitāḥ homam havyam hutam dānam deyam dātā tapaḥ śamaḥ dhruvam sthānam vidhānam ca niyamaḥ ca iti viṃśatiḥ mukhyāḥ hi ete samākhyātāḥ sāvarṇe prathame antare mārīcasya eva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ nava ca anyeṣu vakṣyāmi sāvarṇeḥ ca antareṣu vai sāvarṇa manavaḥ ca anye bhaviṣyāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ dakṣasya te hi dauhitrāḥ priyāyāḥ duhituḥ sutāḥ mahatā tapasā yuktāḥ meru pṛṣṭe mahā ojasaḥ brahma ādibhiḥ te janitāḥ dakṣeṇa eva ca dhīmatā mahar loka gatāḥ āvṛtya bhaviṣyāḥ merum āśritāḥ mahābhāvāt tu te pūrvam jajñire cākṣuṣe antare sāvarṇāḥ nāmataḥ pañca catvāraḥ parama ṛṣi jāḥ saṃjñā putraḥ tu sāvarṇaḥ ekaḥ vaivasvataḥ tathā jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃjñā sutaḥ nāma manuḥ vaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ caturddaśā ete manavaḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrtti varddhanāḥ vede śrutau purāṇe ca sarve te prabhaviṣṇavaḥ prajānām patayaḥ sarve bhūtānām patayaḥ sthitāḥ taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sa parvatā pūrṇam yuga sahasram vai paripālyā nareśvaraiḥ caturddaśā eva te jñeyāḥ sargāḥ svāyambhuva ādayaḥ vinivṛtta adhikārāḥ te mahar lokam samāśritāḥ samatītāḥ tu ye teṣām aṣṭau ṣaṣṭāḥ tathā apare pūrveṣu sāmprataḥ ca ayam śāntiḥ vaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ ye śiṣṭāḥ tān pravakṣyāmi saha deva ṛṣi dānavaiḥ saha prajā nisargeṇa sarvvān tu anāgatān dvijān vaivasvata nisargeṇa teṣām jñeyaḥ tu vistaraḥ anyūnāḥ na atiriktāḥ te yasmāt sarvve vivasvataḥ kule kule nisargān tu tasmāt bhūyas vibhāgaśaḥ teṣām eva hi śiṣṭa artham vistareṇa krameṇa ca dakṣasya kanyā dharmiṣṭā suvratā nāma viśrutā gṛhītvā tām pitā kanyām jagāma brahmaṇaḥ antike bhava dharma samīpa stham dakṣam brahmā abyabhāṣata caturaḥ vai manūn putrān cāturvarṇya karān śubhān tām kanyām manasā jagmuḥ trayaḥ te brahmaṇā saha satya abhidhyāyinām teṣām sadyas kanyā vyajāyata sadṛśa anurūpān teṣām caturaḥ vai kumārakān saṃsiddhāḥ kārya karaṇe sambhūtāḥ te śriyā anvitaḥ te dṛṣṭvā tān svayam buddhvā brahmā yasya yaḥ sadṛśaḥ ca api rūpe ca nāmataḥ tam gṛhṇātu su bhadram vaḥ varṇataḥ yasya yaḥ samaḥ tasmāt ātma samaḥ putraḥ pituḥ mātuḥ ca jāyate evam te samayam kṛtvā savarṇān jagṛhuḥ sutān cākṣuṣasya antare atīte prāpte vaivasvatasya ha vaivasvataḥ manuḥ yaḥ ca sāvarṇaḥ yaḥ ca viśrutaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃjñā sutaḥ vidvān manuḥ vaivasvataḥ prabhuḥ savarṇāyāḥ sutaḥ ca anyaḥ smṛtaḥ vaivasvataḥ manuḥ savarṇāḥ manavaḥ ye ca catvāraḥ tu mahā ṛṣi jāḥ tapasā sambhṛta ātmānaḥ sveṣu manvantareṣu vai bhaviṣyeṣu bhaviṣyanti sarva kārya artha sādhakāḥ putrāḥ marīcigarbhāḥ ca suśarmāṇaḥ ca te trayaḥ bhaviṣyasya bhaviṣyaḥ tu ekaikaḥ dvādaśaḥ gaṇaḥ aiśvarya saṃgrāhaḥ rāhaḥ bāhu vaśaḥ tathā eva ca pārāḥ dvādaśa vijñeyāḥ uttarān tu nibodhata dadhi krāvāya pakvāḥ ca praṇītaḥ vijayaḥ madhuḥ suśarmmāṇaḥ tu vakṣyāmi nāmataḥ tu nibodhata sunemiḥ dyutapāḥ ca eva suśarmmāṇaḥ prakīrttitāḥ teṣām indraḥ tadā bhāvyaḥ hi adbhutaḥ nāma nāmataḥ skandaḥ soma pratīkāśaḥ kārtikeyaḥ tu pāvakaḥ māghātithiḥ ca paulastyaḥ vasuḥ kāśyapaḥ eva ca jyotiṣmān bhārgavaḥ ca eva dyutimān aṅgirāḥ tathā vasitaḥ ca eva vāsiṣṭhaḥ ātreyaḥ havyavāhanaḥ dhṛtiketu dīptiketu śāpahastāḥ nirāmayaḥ pṛthuśravāḥ tathā nākaḥ bhūridyumnaḥ bṛhadrathaḥ prathamasya tu sāvarṇeḥ nava putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ sukha amanāḥ viruddhāḥ ca dvau eva tu gaṇau smṛtau tviṣivantaḥ ca te sarve śata saṅkhyāḥ ca te samāḥ prāṇāḥ proktaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ puruṣeṣu vai teṣām indraḥ tathā vidvān bhaviṣyaḥ śāntiḥ ucyate haviṣmān paulahaḥ śrīmān sukīrtiḥ ca api bhārgavaḥ āpomūrtiḥ tathā ātreyaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca api yaḥ smṛtaḥ paulastyaḥ pratipaḥ ca api nābhāgaḥ ca eva kāśyapaḥ abhimanyuḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ saptā ete parama ṛṣayaḥ sukṣetraḥ ca uttamaujāḥ ca bhūriṣeṇaḥ ca vīryavān śatānīkaḥ nirāmitraḥ vṛṣasenaḥ jayadrathaḥ bhūridyumnaḥ suvarccāḥ ca daśā ete mānavāḥ smṛtāḥ ekādaśe tu paryyāye sāvarṇe vai tṛtīyake nirmmāṇa ratayaḥ devāḥ kāma jāḥ vai manaḥ javāḥ gaṇāḥ tu ete trayaḥ khyātāḥ devatānām mahātmanām ekaikam triṃśataḥ teṣām gaṇāḥ tu tridivaukasām māsasya ahāni triṃśat tu yāni vai kavayaḥ viduḥ nirmmāṇa ratayaḥ devāḥ rātrayaḥ tu vihaṅgamāḥ gaṇāḥ te vai trayaḥ proktāḥ devatānām bhaviṣyati manojavāḥ muhūrttāḥ tu iti devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ete hi brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ bhaviṣyāḥ manavaḥ smṛtāḥ teṣām indraḥ vṛṣaḥ nāma bhaviṣyaḥ surarāj tatas teṣām saptarṣayaḥ ca api kīrttyamānān nibodhata haviṣmān kāśyapaḥ ca api vapuṣmān yaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ vāruṇiḥ ca eva ca ātreyaḥ vāsiṣṭaḥ bhagaḥ eva ca puṣṭiḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ jñeyaḥ paulastyaḥ niścaraḥ tathā sarvvavegaḥ sudharmmā ca devānīkaḥ purovahaḥ kṣemadharmā gṛheṣuḥ ca hi ādarśaḥ pauṇḍrakaḥ manaḥ sāvarṇasya tu te putrāḥ prājāpatyasya vai manoḥ caturthe ṛtusāvarṇe devāḥ tasya antare śrṛṇu pañca eva tu gaṇāḥ proktāḥ devatānām anāgatāḥ haritāḥ rohitāḥ ca eva devāḥ sumanasaḥ tathā parvatānucaraḥ ca eva hi apoṃśuḥ ca manojavaḥ urjjā svāhā svadhā tārā daśā ete rohitāḥ smṛtāḥ tapaḥ jā nirbhṛtiḥ ca eva vācā bandhuḥ ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ vyuṣṭiḥ vidhiḥ ca vai devaḥ daśā ete rohitāḥ smṛtāḥ uṣita ādyāḥ tu ye devāḥ trayastriśat prakīrtitāḥ suparvā vṛṣabhaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṛpi dyumnau vipaścitaḥ śubhaḥ havikṛtāt prāptiḥ vyāpṛthaḥ daśamaḥ tathā supārāḥ mānasāḥ tu ete devāḥ vai samprakīrttitāḥ teṣām indraḥ tu vijñeyaḥ ṛta dhāmā mahā yaśāḥ kṛtiḥ vasiṣṭha putraḥ tu hi ātreyaḥ sutapāḥ tathā tapomūrtiḥ ca āṅgirasaḥ tapasvī kāśyapaḥ tathā tapaḥ śayānaḥ paulastyaḥ pulahaḥ ca tapaḥ ratiḥ bhārgavaḥ saptamaḥ tu eṣām vijñeyaḥ tu tapomatiḥ devavān upadevaḥ ca devaśreṣṭaḥ vidūrathaḥ mitrabāhuḥ suvarcāḥ ca dvādaśā ete manoḥ sutāḥ trayaḥ daśe tu paryāye bhāvyāḥ raucya antare punar trayaḥ eva gaṇāḥ proktāḥ devānām tu svayambhuvā brahmaṇaḥ mānasāḥ putrāḥ te hi sarve mahātmanaḥ su trāmāṇaḥ sudharmmāṇaḥ su karmmāṇaḥ ca te trayaḥ tridaśānām gaṇāḥ proktāḥ bhaviṣyāḥ soma pāyinaḥ trayastriṃśat devatāḥ yāḥ prābhaviṣyanta yājñikaiḥ ājyena pṛṣadājyena graha śreṣṭena ca eva hi sutrāmāṇaḥ prayājyāḥ tu sāmpratam sukarmaṇaḥ anuyājyāḥ tu pṛṣadājya āśinaḥ tu ye upayājyāḥ sudharmāṇaḥ iti devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ pulaha ātmaja putrāḥ te vijñeyāḥ tu ruceḥ sutāḥ aṅgirāḥ ca eva dhṛtimān paulastyaḥ pathyavān tu saḥ svarūpaḥ ca eva vāsiṣṭhaḥ saptā ete tu trayodaśe devatānām gaṇāḥ pañca proktāḥ ye tu bhaviṣyati vācāvṛddhāḥ ca iti ete pañca deva gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ bṛhat ādyāni sāmāni kaniṣṭān sapta tān viduḥ sapta lokāḥ paritrāste bhājirāḥ sapta sindhavaḥ vācāvṛddhān ṛṣīn viddhi manoḥ svāyambhuvasya vai sarve manvantara indrāḥ ca vijñeyāḥ tulya lakṣaṇāḥ tejasā tapasā buddhyā bala śruta parākramaiḥ bhūta apavādinaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ madhyasthāḥ bhūta vādinaḥ bhūta anuvādinaḥ saktāḥ trayaḥ vedāḥ pravādinām agnidhraḥ kāśyapaḥ ca eva paulastyaḥ māgadhaḥ ca yaḥ bhārgavaḥ hi agnibāhuḥ ca śuciḥ āṅgirasaḥ tathā savarṇāḥ manavaḥ hi ete catvāraḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ niḥśeṣeṣu ca sarveṣu tadā manvantareṣu iha tatas sthānāni śūnyāni sthāninām tāni vai dvijāḥ prabhraśyanti vimuktāni tārā ṛkṣa grahaiḥ tathā sa indra aṣṭeṣu mahar lokam yasmin te kalpa vāsinaḥ tatas teṣu gateṣu ūrddhvam sā āyojyam kalpa vāsinām sa śarīrāḥ ca śrūyante jana lokam saha anugāḥ evam deveṣu atīteṣu mahar lokāt janam prati bhūta ādiṣu avaśiṣṭeṣu sthāvara anteṣu ca api uta śūnyeṣu lokasthāneṣu mahānteṣu bhūḥ ādiṣu deveṣu ca gateṣu ūrddhvam sā āyojyam kalpa vāsinām saṃhṛtya tān tatas brahmā deva ṛṣi pitṛ dānavān saṃsthāpayati vai sargam mahat ṝṣṭyā yuga kṣaye rātrim yuga sahasra antām ahorātra vidaḥ janāḥ trividhaḥ sarvva bhūtānām iti eṣa pratisañcaraḥ pratisarge tu bhūtānām prākṛtaḥ karaṇa kṣayaḥ jñānāt ca ātyantikaḥ proktaḥ kāraṇānām asambhavaḥ tatas saṃhṛtya tān brahmā devān trailokya vāsinaḥ suṣupsuḥ bhagavān brahmā prajāḥ saṃharate tadā tatra ātma sthāḥ prajāḥ karttum prapede sa prajāpatiḥ tadā bhavati anāvṛṣṭiḥ tadā sā śata vārṣikī tathā yāni alpa sārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivī tale sapta raśmiḥ atho bhūtvā hi udatiṣṭhat vibhāvasuḥ haritāḥ raśmayaḥ tasya dīpyamānāḥ tu saptabhiḥ bhaumam kāṣṭham dhanam tejaḥ bhṛśam adbhiḥ tu dīpyate na avṛṣṭyā tapate sūryaḥ na avṛṣṭyā pariviṣyate na avṛṣṭyā paricinvanti vāriṇā dīpyate raviḥ tena āhāreṇa sandīptaḥ sūryaḥ sapta bhavati uta tatas te raśmayaḥ sapta sūryya bhūtāḥ caturdiśam prāpnuvanti ca bhābhiḥ tu hi ūrddham ca adhas ca raśmibhiḥ dīpyante bhāskarāḥ sapta yuga anta agniḥ pratāpinaḥ te vāriṇā ca saṃdīptāḥ bahu sāhasra raśmayaḥ tatas teṣām pratāpena dahyamānā vasundharā sa adri nadī arṇavā pṛthvī visnehā samapadyata dīptābhiḥ santatābhiḥ ca citrābhiḥ ca samantataḥ sūrya agnīnām pravṛddhānām saṃsṛṣṭānām parasparam sarva loka praṇāśañca saḥ agniḥ bhūtvā tu maṇḍalī tatas pralīyate sarvvam jaṅgamam sthāvaram tadā nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmiḥ kūrma pṛṣṭha samā bhavet ambarīṣam iva ābhāti sarvam māriṣitam jagat sarvam eva tadā arcirbhiḥ pūrṇam jajvālyate nabhaḥ pātāle yāni bhūtāni ca dvīpāḥ ca parvatāḥ ca eva varṣāṇi atha mahā udadhiḥ tatas saṃvarttakaḥ śailān atikramya mahān tathā tatas sa pṛthivīm bhittvā rasātalam aśoṣayat nirdahya tān tu pātālān nāga lokam atha adahat adhastāt pṛthivīm dagdhvā hi ūrddhvam sa dahate divam yojanānām sahasrāṇi hi ayutāni arbudāni ca gandharvān ca piśācān ca sa mahā uraga rākṣasān ghoram dahati kālāgniḥ evam loka catuṣṭayam vyāpteṣu teṣu lokeṣu tiryak ūrddhvam atha agninā tat tejaḥ samanuprāptam kṛtsnam jagat idam śanais ayaḥ guḍa nibham sarvvam tadā hi evam prakāśate tatas gaja kula ākārāḥ taḍidbhiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ uttiṣṭhanti tadā ghorāḥ vyomni saṃvarttakāḥ ghanāḥ kecid nīlotpala śyāmāḥ kecid kumuda sannibhāḥ kecid vaiḍhūrya saṃkāśāḥ indranīla nibhā apare śaṅkha kunda nibhāḥ ca anye jāti añjana nibhāḥ tathā dhūmra varṇāḥ ghanāḥ kecid kecid pītāḥ payodharāḥ kecid rāsabha varṇa ābhāḥ lākṣā rakta nibhāḥ tathā manaḥśilā ābhāḥ tu apare kapota ābhāḥ tathā ambudāḥ kecid pura dhara ākārāḥ kecid gaja kula upamāḥ ke cit parvata saṃkāśāḥ kecid sthala nibhāḥ ghanāḥ kuṇḍāgāra nibhāḥ kecid kecid mīna kula upamāḥ bahu rūpāḥ ghora rūpāḥ ghora svara ninādinaḥ tatas te jaladāḥ ghorāḥ navīnāḥ bhāskara ātmikāḥ saptadhā saṃvṛta ātmānaḥ tam agnim śamayanti uta su ghoram aśivam sarvvam nāśayanti ca pāvakam pravṛṣṭaiḥ ca tathā atyartham vāribhiḥ pūryyate jagat adbhiḥ tejaḥ abhibhūtam ca tadā agniḥ prāviśati apaḥ naṣṭe ca agnau varṣa śate payodāḥ pāka sambhavāḥ dhārābhiḥ pūrayanti imam codyamānāḥ svayambhuvā saṃveṣṭayati ghora ātmā divi vāyuḥ samantataḥ tasmin ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame pūrṇe yuga sahasre vai niḥśeṣaḥ kalpaḥ ucyate atha ambhasā vṛte loke prāhuḥ ekārṇavam budhāḥ atha bhūmi talam vāyuḥ ca ekārṇave tadā pārthivāḥ tu atha sāmudrāḥ āpaḥ haimāḥ ca sarvvaśas āgatāgatikam ca eva tadā tat salilam smṛtam pracchādya tiṣṭhati mahīm arṇava ākhyam ca tat jalam ābhānti yasmāt tāḥ bhābhiḥ bhā śabda vyāpti dīptiṣu ekārṇave tadā yaḥ vai na śīghrāḥ tena tāḥ narāḥ tāvantam kālam evam tu bhavati ekārṇavam jagat tadā tu sarvva vyāpārāḥ nivarttante prajāpateḥ evam ekārṇave tasmin naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame tadā sa bhavati brahmā sahasra akṣaḥ sahasra pād sahasra śīrṣā sumanāḥ sahasra pād sahasra cakṣuḥ vadanaḥ sahasra vāc āditya varṇaḥ bhuvanasya goptā hi apūrvaḥ ekaḥ prathamaḥ turāṣāh suṣupsuḥ aprakāśām svām rātrim tu kurute prabhuḥ caturvidhāḥ yadā śete prajāḥ sarvva aṇḍa maṇḍitāḥ paśyante tam mahātmānam kālam sapta mahā ṛṣayaḥ bhṛgu ādayaḥ mahātmānaḥ pūrve vyākhyāta lakṣaṇāḥ satya ādīn sapta lokān vai te hi paśyanti cakṣuṣā brahmāṇam te tu paśyanti mahā brāhmīṣu rātriṣu saptarṣayaḥ prapaśyanti sapta kālam sva rātriṣu kalpānām parameṣṭi tvāt tasmāt ādyaḥ sa paṭyate sa yaṣṭā sarva bhūtānām kalpa ādiṣu punar punar evam āveśayitvā tu sva ātmani eva prajāpatiḥ atha ātmani mahā tejāḥ sarvam ādāya sarva kṛt manaḥ sisṛkṣayā yuktam sargāya nidadhe punar dehaiḥ viyogaḥ satvānām tasmin vai kṛtsnaśas smṛtaḥ tatas dagdheṣu bhūteṣu sarvveṣu āditya raśmibhiḥ gandharva ādīni satvāni piśāca antāni sarvvaśas tadā tāni api dagdhāni dhuta pāpāni sarvvaśas vyuṣṭāyāntu rajanyām tu brahmaṇe avyakta yonaye jāyante hi punar tāni sarvva bhūtāni kṛtsnaśas ṛṣayaḥ manavaḥ devāḥ prajāḥ sarvvaḥ caturvidhāḥ teṣām api iha siddhānām nidhana utpattiḥ ucyate tathā janma nirodhaḥ ca bhūtānām iha dṛśyate ā bhūtasaṃplavāt tasmāt bhavaḥ saṃsāraḥ ucyate yathā sarvvāṇi bhūtāni jāyante hi varṣāsu iha sthāvara ādīni sattvāni kalpe kalpe tathā prajāḥ yathā ārttau ṛtu liṅgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryaye dṛśyante tāni tāni eva tathā brahmāttarātriṣu niṣkramante viśante ca prajā kāram prajāpatim brahmāṇam sarva bhūtāni mahā yogam maheśvaram saṃsraṣṭā sarva bhūtānām kalpa ādiṣu punar punar yena eva sṛṣṭāḥ prathamam prayātāḥ āpaḥ hi mārgeṇa mahī tale asmin ye ca api devāḥ manavaḥ prajā īśāḥ anye api ye svarga gatāḥ ca siddhāḥ sat bhāvita ākhyāti vaśāt ca dharmmyāḥ punar nisargeṇa bhavanti sattvāḥ atas ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi kālam ābhūtasaṃplavam manvantarāṇi yāni syuḥ vyākhyātāni mayā dvijāḥ sa yuga ākhyā sahasram tu sarvāṇi eva antarāṇi vai asyāḥ sahasre dve pūrṇe niḥśeṣaḥ kalpaḥ ucyate nimeṣaḥ tulya mātrā hi kṛtaḥ laghu akṣareṇa tu mānuṣa akṣi nimeṣāḥ tu kāṣṭā pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ lavaḥ kṣaṇāḥ tu pañca eva viṃśat kāṣṭā tu te trayaḥ prasthaḥ sapta udakāḥ ca eva sādhikāḥ tu lavaḥ smṛtaḥ lavāḥ triṃśat kalāḥ muhūrtaḥ triṃśataḥ kalāḥ ahorātram kalānām tu vyadhikāni śatāni ṣaḍ tāḥ ca eva saṃkhyāyāḥ jñeyam candra āditya gatiḥ yathā nimeṣāḥ daśa pañca eva kāṣṭāḥ tāḥ triṃśataḥ kalāḥ triṃśat kalā muhūrttaḥ tu daśa bhāgaḥ kalā smṛtā catvāriṃśat kalānām tu muhūrttaḥ iti saṃjñataḥ muhūrttāḥ ca lavāḥ ca api pramāṇa jñaiḥ prakalpitāḥ tad sthāne na ambhasāḥ ca api palāni atha trayodaśa ete ca api udakaprasthāḥ catvāraḥ nālikaḥ dhaṭaḥ hema māṣaiḥ kṛta chidraiḥ caturbhiḥ catur aṅgulaiḥ raveḥ gati viśeṣeṇa sarveṣu nṛṣu nityaśas tat ahar mānuṣam jñeyam nākṣatram tu daśa adhikam sāvanena tu māsena hi abdaḥ ayam mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ahnā anena tu yā saṃkhyā māsa ṛtu ayana vārṣikī tadā baddham idam jñānam saṃjñā yā hi upalakṣyatām kalānām su parīmāṇāt kālaḥ iti abhidhīyate yat ahar brahmaṇaḥ proktam divyā koṭī tu tat smṛta śatānām ca sahasrāṇi ca navatiṃca sahasrāṇi tathā eva anyāni yāni tu saṃsthā sambhajanam jñānam apṛcchan antaram tadā saṃplāvanasya mānuṣeṇa eva sammatam mānena śrotum icchāmaḥ saṃkṣepa artha pada akṣaram teṣām śrutvā sa devaḥ tu vāyuḥ loka hite rataḥ saṃkṣepāt divya cakṣuṣmān provāca bhagavān prabhuḥ tāsām saṅkhyāya varṣa agram brāhyam vakṣyāmi ahar kṣaye koṭi śatāni catvāri varṣāṇi mānuṣāṇi tu dvātriṃśat ca tathā koṭyaḥ saṅkhyātāḥ saṅkhyayā dvijaiḥ tathā śata sahasrāṇi ekonanavatiḥ punar āśītiḥ ca sahasrāṇi eṣa kālaḥ plavasya tu mānuṣa ākhyeṇa saṅkhyātaḥ kālaḥ hi ā bhūta saṃplavaḥ sapta sūryāḥ tadā agreṣu tadā lokeṣu teṣu vai mahābhūteṣu līyante prajāḥ sarvvāḥ caturvidhāḥ vinivṛtte ca saṃhāre upaśānte prajāpatau īśvara dhiṣṭite hi asmin tadā hi ekārṇave tadā tāvat ekārṇavaḥ jñeyaḥ yāvat āsīt ahar prabhoḥ rātriḥ tu salila avasthā nivṛttau ca api ahar samṛtam ābhūtasaṃplavaḥ hi eṣa ahorātraḥ smṛtaḥ prabhoḥ ābhūtebhyaḥ pralīyante tasmāt ābhūtasaṃplavaḥ ābhūtaḥ plavate ca eva tasmāt ābhūtasaṃplavaḥ atītāḥ varttamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ prajāḥ divya saṅkhyā prasaṅkhyātā hi aparārdha guṇīkṛtā parārdha dviguṇañca api parama āyuḥ prakīrttitam yathā vāyu pravegena dīpa arciḥ upaśāmyati tathā hi apratisaṃsṛṣṭe mahat ādau maheśvare iti eṣa ca samākhyātaḥ mayā hi ābhūtasaṃplavaḥ samāsena samākhyātaḥ bhūyas kim varttayāmi vaḥ yaḥ idam dhārayet nityam śrṛṇuyāt vā api abhīkṣṇaśas kīrttanāt śravaṇāt ca api mahatīm siddhim āpnuyāt asādhāraṇa vṛttaiḥ tu hutaśeṣa ādibhiḥ dvijaiḥ dharmma vaiśeṣikaiḥ ca eva hi ācūrṇa sūkṣma darśibhiḥ caturddaśā ete manavaḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrtti vardhanāḥ atītāḥ varttamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ ca ye sarvve hi api krama atītāḥ mahar lokam samāśritāḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ dhārmikaiḥ sahitaiḥ surāḥ sarvve hi api krama atītāḥ mahar lokam samāśritāḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ dhārmikaiḥ sahitaiḥ surāḥ varṇa āśramāṇām dharmmeṣu śrauta smārtteṣu saṃsthitaiḥ vinivṛtta adhikārāḥ te yāvat manvantara kṣayaḥ caturddaśa eva sthānāni varṇitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ loka ākhyāni tu yāni syuḥ yeṣu tiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ sapta teṣu kṛtāni āhuḥ akṛtāni tu sapta vai bhūḥ ādayaḥ tu saṅkhyātāḥ sapta lokāḥ kṛtāḥ tu iha akṛtāni tu sapta eva prākṛtāni tu yāni vai sthānāni sthānibhiḥ sārddham kṛtāni tu nibandhanam pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca divyam yat ca mahaḥ smṛtam sthānāni etāni catvāri smṛtāni ārṇavakāni ca kṣaya atiśaya yuktāni tathā yuktāni vakṣyate yāni naimittikāni syuḥ tiṣṭhanti ābhūtasaṃplavam janaḥ tapaḥ ca satyam ca sthānāni etāni trīṇi tu aikāntikāni sattvāni tiṣṭhanti iha a prasaṃyamāt bhūrlokaḥ prathamaḥ teṣām dvitīyaḥ tu bhuvaḥ smṛtaḥ svaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ caturthaḥ vai mahaḥ smṛtaḥ janaḥ tu pañcamaḥ lokaḥ tapaḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ vibhāvyate bhūḥ iti vyāhṛte pūrvam bhūḥ lokaḥ ca tatas abhavat tṛtīyam svar iti iti ukte divam prādurbabhūva ha tṛtīyam svar iti iti ukte divam prādurbabhūva ha bhūtasya adhipatiḥ ca agniḥ tatas bhūtapatiḥ smṛtaḥ vinivṛtta adhikārāṇām devānām tatra vai kṣayaḥ tāsām svāyaṃbhuva ādyānām prajānām jananāt janaḥ yāḥ tāḥ svāyambhuva ādyāḥ hi purastāt parikīrttitāḥ ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāra ādyāḥ yatra santi ūrddhvaretasaḥ tapasā bhāvitātmānaḥ tatra santi iti vā tapaḥ satya iti brahmaṇaḥ śabdaḥ sattā mātraḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ yakṣāḥ guhyakāḥ tu sarākṣasāḥ sarva bhūta piśācāḥ ca nāgāḥ ca saha mānuṣaiḥ marutaḥ mātariśvānaḥ rudrāḥ devāḥ tathā aśvinau ādityāḥ ṛbhavaḥ viśve sādhyāḥ ca pitaraḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ aṅgirasaḥ ca eva bhuvar lokam samāśritāḥ ete vaimānikāḥ devāḥ tārāgraha nivāsinaḥ iti ete kramaśas proktāḥ brahma vyāhāra sambhavāḥ bhūrloka prathamāḥ lokāḥ mahat antāḥ ca te smṛtāḥ ārabhyante tu tanmātraiḥ śuddhāḥ teṣām parasparam śukra ādyāḥ cākṣuṣa antāḥ ca ye vyatītāḥ bhuvam śritāḥ bhūrloka prathamāḥ lokāḥ mahat antāḥ ca ye smṛtāḥ marīciḥ kaśyapaḥ dakṣaḥ tathā svāyambhuvaḥ aṅgirāḥ ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāra ādyāḥ vairājyāḥ te tapodhanāḥ manvantarāṇām sarveṣām sāvarṇānām tatas smṛtāḥ caturddaśānām sarveṣām punarāvṛtti hetavaḥ yogam tapaḥ ca satyam ca samādhāya tad ātmani brahma lokaḥ samākhyātaḥ hi apratīghāta lakṣaṇaḥ paryāsa pārimāṇyena bhūrlokaḥ samitiḥ smṛtaḥ bhūmi antaram yat ādityāt antarikṣam bhuvaḥ smṛtam vikhyātāḥ sapta lokāḥ tu teṣām vakṣyāmi siddhayaḥ bhūrloka vāsinaḥ sarve hi anna ādāḥ tu rama ātmakāḥ vijñeyā mānasī teṣām siddhiḥ vai pañca lakṣaṇā prathama anantaraiḥ iṣṭvā hi antarāḥ sāmprataiḥ punar vinivṛtta adhikārāṇām siddhiḥ teṣām tu mānasī teṣām tu mānasī jñeyā śuddhā siddhi paramparā uktāḥ lokāḥ ca catvāraḥ janasya anuvidhiḥ tathā samāsena mayā viprāḥ bhūyas tam varttayāmi vaḥ marīciḥ kaśyapaḥ dakṣaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ pūrvam te saṃprasūyante brahmaṇaḥ manasā iha tatas prajāḥ pratiṣṭāpya janam eva āśrayanti te kalpa dāha pradīpteṣu tadā kāleṣu teṣu vai bhūrā diṣu mahānteṣu bhṛśam vyāpteṣu atha agninā śikhā saṃvarttakā jñeyā prāpnuvanti sadā janāḥ yāma ādayaḥ gaṇāḥ sarve mahar loka nivāsinaḥ teṣām te tulya sāmarthyāḥ tulya mūrtti dharāḥ tathā vyuṣṭā āyāntu rajanyām vai brahmaṇaḥ avyakta yoninaḥ svāyambhuva ādayaḥ sarve marīci antāḥ tu sādhakāḥ devāḥ te vai punar teṣām jāyante nidhaneṣu iha yāma ādayaḥ krameṇa eva kaniṣṭa ādyāḥ prajāpateḥ pūrvam pūrvam prasūyante paścime paścacimāḥ tathā deva anvaye devatāḥ hi sapta sambhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ vyatītāḥ kalya jāḥ teṣām tisraḥ śiṣṭāḥ tathā pare āvarttamānāḥ devāḥ te krameṇa ete na sarvvaśas gatvā punar punar tatas te vai gaṇāḥ sarvve dṛṣṭvā bhāveṣu anitya tām īhā utpannāḥ tatas te vai sthānā āpūrayanti uta evam deva gaṇāḥ sarve daśa kṛtvas nivarttya vai vairājeṣu upapannāḥ te daśa tiṣṭhanti upaplavān pūrṇe pūrṇe tatas kalpe sthitvā vairājake punar evam deva yugāni iha vyatītāni sahasraśas nidhanam brahma loke tu gatānām ṛṣibhiḥ saha na śakyam ānupūrveṇa teṣām vaktum pravistaram anādi tvāt ca kālasya hi asam khyānāt ca sarvaśas tat upaśrutya vākya artham ṛṣayaḥ saṃśaya anvitāḥ sūtam āhuḥ purāṇa jñam vyāsa śiṣyam mahā matim vairājāḥ te yad āhārāḥ yad sattvāḥ ca yad āśrayāḥ tat uktam ṛṣibhiḥ vākyam śrutvā loka artha tattva vid sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ vākyam vinayena idam abravīt ābhūta saṃplavāḥ tatra daśa tiṣṭhanti tejanāḥ sarve sūkṣma śarīrāḥ te vidvāṃsaḥ ghana mūrttayaḥ sthita loka asthita tvāt ca teṣām bhūtam na vidyate ūcuḥ sanatkumāra ādyāḥ siddhāḥ te thoga dharmiṇaḥ evam eva mahābhāgāḥ praṇavam sampraviśya ha tatra eva sampralīyante śāntāḥ dīpa arciṣaḥ yathā ānandam brahmaṇaḥ prāpya hi amṛta tvāya te gatāḥ ānandam brahmaṇaḥ prāpya amṛta tvam ca bhajanti uta ādhipatyam vinā tulyāḥ brahmaṇaḥ te mahā ojasaḥ tapasaḥ ante kriyā ātmānaḥ buddha avasthāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ avyakte saṃpralīyante sarve te kṣaṇa darśinaḥ apunarmārga ga ādīnām teṣām ca eva ūrddhvaretasām karma abhyāsa kṛtā śuddhiḥ vedānteṣu upalakṣyate tatra te abhyāsinaḥ yuktāḥ parām kāṣṭām upāsate hitvā śarīram pāpmānam amṛta tvāya te gatāḥ vīta rāgāḥ jita krodhāḥ nirmohāḥ satya vādinaḥ śāntāḥ praṇihita ātmānaḥ dayāvantaḥ jita indriyāḥ niḥsaṅgāḥ śucayaḥ ca eva brahma sāyujya gāḥ smṛtāḥ teṣām abhraṃśinaḥ lokāḥ aprameya sukhāḥ smṛtāḥ kasmāt eṣa parārddhaḥ ca kaḥ ca eṣa paraḥ ucyate śrṛṇudhvam me parārddham ca parisaṃkhyām parasya ca evam daśa śatam ca eva sahasram ca eva saṅkhyayā sahasrāṇi daśa ayutam tathā śata sahasrāṇām arbudam koṭiḥ ucyate arbudam daśa koṭyaḥ tu hi abjam koṭi śatam viduḥ sahasram api koṭīnām kharvam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ daśa koṭi sahasrāṇi nikharvam iti tam viduḥ śatam koṭi sahasrāṇām saṅkuḥ iti abhidhīyate koṭi sahasra srāṇām koṭīnām daśadhā punar guṇitāni samudram vai prāhuḥ saṃkhyā vidaḥ janāḥ parārddhaḥ iti kīrtyate parārddha dviguṇam ca api param āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ śatam āhuḥ paridṛḍham sahasram paripadmakam vijñeyam ayutam tasmāt niyutam prayutam tatas evam aṣṭādaśa etāni sthānāni gaṇanā vidhau śatāni iti vijānīyāt saṃjñitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ kalpa saṃkhyā pravṛttasya parārddham brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam paraḥ eṣa parārddhan ca saṃkhyātaḥ saṃkhyayā mayā yasmāt asya param vīryam parama āyuḥ parantapaḥ parā śaktiḥ paraḥ dharmmaḥ parā vidyā parā dhṛtiḥ saṃkhyātaḥ tu paraḥ brahmā tasya arddham tu parārddha tā saṃkhyeyam ca api asaṃkhyeyam satatam ca api tam trikam saṃkhyeyam saṃkhyayā dṛṣṭam apāra arddhāt vibhāṣyate rāśau dṛṣṭe na saṃkhyā asti tat asaṃkhyasya lakṣaṇam ānantyam sikatā ākhyeṣu dṛṣṭavān pañca lakṣaṇam īśvaraiḥ tat prasaṃkhyātam śuddha tvāt divya dṛṣṭibhiḥ evam jñāna pratiṣṭha tvāt sarvvam brahma anupaśyati bāṣpa paryyākula akṣāḥ tu praharṣāt ghadghada svarāḥ yojana agreṇa saṃkhyātaḥ sādhanam yojanasya tu krośasya ca parīmāṇam śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā mātariśvā vinīta vāc uvāca madhuram vākyam yathādṛṣṭam yathākramam etat vaḥ aham pravakṣyāmi śrṛṇudhvam me vivakṣitam daśa eva mahatām bhāgāḥ bhūtādiḥ sthūlaḥ ucyate daśa bhāga adhikam ca api bhūtādiḥ paramāṇukaḥ paramāṇuḥ su sūkṣmaḥ tu bā avagrāhyaḥ na cakṣuṣā jāla antara gatam bhānoḥ yat sūkṣmam dṛśyate rajaḥ prathamam tad pramāṇānām paramāṇum pracakṣate aṣṭānām paramāṇūnām samavāyaḥ yadā bhavet trasareṇavaḥ ca ye api aṣṭau rathareṇuḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ te api aṣṭau samavāya sthāḥ bālāgram tat smṛtam budhaiḥ bālāgrāṇi aṣṭa likṣā syāt yūkā tat ca aṣṭakam bhavet yūka aṣṭakam yavam prāhuḥ aṅgulam tu yavāṣṭakam dvādaśa aṅgula parvvāṇi vitasti sthānam ucyate ratniḥ ca aṅgula parvāṇi vijñeyaḥ hi ekaviṃśatiḥ catvāri viṃśatiḥ ca eva hastaḥ syāt aṅgulāni tu kiṣkuḥ dvi ratniḥ vijñeyaḥ dvicatvāriṃśat aṅgulaḥ ṣaṇṇavati aṅgulam ca eva dhanuḥ āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ etat gavyūti saṃkhyāyām pādānām dhanuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ dhanuḥ daṇḍaḥ yugam nālī tulyāni etāni atha aṅgulaiḥ dhanuṣaḥ tri śatam nalvam āhuḥ saṃkhyā vidaḥ janāḥ aṣṭau dhanuḥ sahasrāṇi yojanam tu vidhīyate etat sahasram vijñeyam śakra krośa antaram tathā yojanānām tu saṃkhyātam saṃkhyā jñāna viśāradaiḥ etena yojana agreṇa śrṛṇudhvam brahmaṇaḥ antaram mahī talāt sahasrāṇām śatāt ūrddhvam divākaraḥ divākarāt sahasreṇa tāvat ūrddhvam niśākaraḥ pūrṇam yojanānām niśākarāt nakṣatra maṇḍalam kṛtsnam upariṣṭāt prakāśate śatam sahasram saṃkhyātaḥ meruḥ dvi guṇitam punar graha antaram atha ekaikam ūrddhvam nakṣatra maṇḍalāt tārā grahāṇām sarvveṣām adhastāt carate budhaḥ tatas bṛhaspatiḥ ca ūrddhvam tasmāt ūrddhvam śanaiścaraḥ ūrddhvam yojanānām śanaiścarāt saptarṣi maṇḍalam kṛtsnam upariṣṭāt prakāśate ṛṣibhiḥ tu sahasrāṇām śatāt ūrddhvam vibhāvyate sarveṣām devayonīnām sthiti hetuḥ smṛtaḥ eka yojana koṭī sā iti evam niścayam gatam yatra te brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ dakṣa ādyāḥ sādhakāḥ smṛtāḥ vairājāḥ yatra te devāḥ bhūta dāha vivarjitāḥ ṣaḍguṇam tu tapolokāt satyaloka antaram smṛtam a punarmāra kāmānām brahma lokaḥ saḥ ucyate yasmāt na cyavate bhūyas brahmāṇam saḥ upāsate eka koṭiḥ yojanānām pañcāśat niyutāni tu ūrddhvam bhāgaḥ tatas aṇḍasya brahma lokāt paraḥ smṛtaḥ caturaḥ ca eva koṭyaḥ tu niyutāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭi ca eṣaḥ arddhaṃśa pracāraḥ asya gati antaḥ ca aparaḥ smṛtaḥ dhrava agram etat vayākhyātam yojana agrāt yathāśrutam adhogatīnām vakṣyāmi bhūtānām sthāna kalpanām kṛmī ca kṛmibhakṣaḥ ca lālābhakṣaḥ viśaṃsanaḥ adhaḥśirāḥ pūyavahaḥ rudhirāndhaḥ tathā eva ca tathā vaitaraṇam kṛṣṇam asipatravanam tathā agnijvālaḥ mahā ghoraḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ atha śvabhojanaḥ tamaḥ ca kṛṣṇasūtraḥ ca lohaḥ ca api asijaḥ tathā apratiṣṭaḥ atha vīci aśva narakāḥ hi evamādayaḥ tāmasāḥ narakāḥ sarve yamasya viṣaye sthitāḥ yeṣu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ patanti iha pṛthak pṛthak bhūmeḥ adhastāt te sarve raurava ādyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ raurave kūṭa sākṣī tu mithyā yaḥ ca abhiśaṃsati krūra grahe pakṣa vādī hi asatyaḥ patate naraḥ yaḥ kuryāt yaḥ ca syāt guru talpa gaḥ taptakumbhī svasā gāmī tathā rāja bhaṭaḥ ca yaḥ mahājvāle duhitaram snuṣām gacchati yaḥ tu vai gurūn ca eva avamanyante vāc krośaiḥ tāḍayanti ca deva brāhmaṇa vidveṣṭā gurūṇām ca api apūjakaḥ paryyaśnāti yaḥ ekaḥ anyaḥ brāhmaṇīm suhṛdaḥ sutām kāṇḍa karttā kulālaḥ ca niṣka harttā cikitsakaḥ ārā meṣu agni dātā yaḥ patate sa viśaṃsane asat pratigrahī yaḥ ca tathā eva a yājya yājakaḥ yaḥ kukkuṭāni badhnāti mārjārān sūkarān ca tān pakṣiṇaḥ ca mṛgān chāgān saḥ api enam narakam vrajet ājīvikaḥ māhiṣakaḥ tathā cakra dhvajī ca yaḥ raṅga upajīvikaḥ vipraḥ śākunigrāma yājakaḥ agāra dāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī soma vikrayī surāpaḥ māṃsa bhakṣaḥ ca tathā ca paśu ghātakaḥ viśa śvastā mahiṣa ādīnām mṛga hantā tathā eva ca parva kāraḥ ca sūcī ca yaḥ ca syāt mitra ghātakaḥ rudhirāndhe patanti ete evam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ mṛṣāvādī naraḥ yaḥ ca tathā prākrośakaḥ aśubhaḥ patet tu narake ghoraḥ mūtra ākīrṇe sa pāpa kṛt madhu grāha abihantāraḥ yanti vaitaraṇīm narāḥ unmattāḥ citta bhagnāḥ ca śauca ācāra vivarjitāḥ krodhanāḥ duḥkha dāḥ ca eva kuhakāḥ kṛṣṭa gāminaḥ karttanaiḥ ca nikṛṣyante mṛga vyādhāḥ su dāruṇaiḥ śabalaiḥ ayastuṇḍaiḥ ca vāyasaiḥ ijyāyām vrata mālopāt sandaṃśe narake patet putraiḥ adhyāpitāḥ ye ca putraiḥ ājñāpitāḥ ca ye varṇa āśrama virūddhāni krodha harṣa samanvitāḥ upariṣṭāt sitaḥ ghoraḥ uṣṇa ātmā rauravaḥ mahān su dāruṇaḥ tu śīta ātmā tasya adhastāt tapaḥ smṛtaḥ bhūmeḥ adhastāt sapta eva narakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ asya adhas punar api anyaḥ śītaḥ tapaḥ iti smṛtaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kālasūtraḥ syāt mahāhavi vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ apratiṣṭhaḥ ścaturthaḥ syāt avīcī pañcamaḥ smṛtaḥ lohapṛṣṭhaḥ tamaḥ teṣām avidheyaḥ tu saptamaḥ ghora tvāt rauravaḥ proktaḥ sa ambhakaḥ dahanaḥ smṛtaḥ su dāruṇaḥ tu śīta ātmā tasya adhastāt tapaḥ adhamaḥ sarpaḥ nikṛntanaḥ proktaḥ kālasūtra iti dāruṇaḥ avīciḥ dāruṇaḥ proktaḥ yantra saṃpīḍanāt ca saḥ tasmāt su dāruṇaḥ lohaḥ karmmaṇām kṣayaṇāt ca saḥ tathābhūtaḥ śarīra tvāt avidhibhyaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ pīḍa bandha vadha āsaṅgāt apratīkāra lakṣaṇaḥ ūrddhvam saila mitāḥ te tu nirālokāḥ ca te smṛtāḥ kūṭa aṅgāra pramāṇaiḥ ca śarīrī mūtra nāyakaḥ duḥkha prakarṣaḥ ca ugra tvam teṣu sarveṣu vai smṛtaḥ yātanāḥ ca api asaṃkhyeyāḥ nārakāṇām tathā smṛtāḥ devāḥ ca nārakāḥ ca eva hi ūrddhvam ca adhas ca saṃsthitāḥ nārakāḥ ca tathā devān sarvān paśyanti adhas mukhān anagra mūla tā yasmāt dhāraṇāḥ ca svabhāvataḥ eṣā svābhāvikī saṃjñā lokāloke pravarttate atha abruvan punar vāyum brāhmaṇāḥ satriṇaḥ tadā sarveṣām eva bhūtānām loka aloka nivāsinām saṃsāre saṃsaranti iha yāvantaḥ prāṇinaḥ ca tān sahkhyayā parisaṅkhyāya tatas prabrūhi kṛtsnaśas ṛṣīṇām tat vacaḥ śrutvā mārutaḥ vākyam abravīt na divya cakṣuṣā jñātum śakyāḥ jñānena vā punar cakṣuṣā vai prasaṃkhyātum atas hi ante narādhipaḥ anādhyānāt avedya tvāt na eva praśnaḥ vidhīyate brahmaṇā saṃjñitam yat tu saṃkhyayā tat nibodhata yaḥ sahasratamaḥ bhāgaḥ sthāvarāṇām bhavet iha pārthivāḥ kṛmayaḥ tāvat saṃseka ādyeṣu sambhavāḥ saṃseka jānām bhāgena sahasreṇa eva sammitāḥ sahasreṇa eva bhāgena satvānām salilaukasām vihaṅgamāḥ tu vijñeyāḥ laukikāḥ te ca sarvaśas yaḥ sahasratamaḥ bhāgaḥ teṣām vai pakṣiṇām bhavet paśavaḥ tad samāḥ jñeyāḥ laukikāḥ tu catuṣpadāḥ catuṣpadānām sarveṣām sahasreṇa eva saṃmatāḥ yaḥ sahasratamaḥ bhāgaḥ dhārmmikāṇām bhavet divi saṃmitāḥ tena bhāgena mokṣiṇaḥ tāvat eva hi svarga upapādakaiḥ tulyā yātanā sthānavāsinaḥ patitāḥ ścūrṇam uddeśāt durātmānaḥ mriyanti ye raurave tāmase hi ete śīta uṣṇam prāpnuvanti te vedanā kaṭuka āstabdhāḥ yātanā sthānam āgatāḥ tatas ghana ātmikaḥ ca api śīta ātmā satatam tapaḥ evam su durlabhāḥ santaḥ svarge ca dhārmmikāḥ narāḥ eṣā saṃkhyā kṛtā saṃkhyā īśvareṇa svayambhuvā gaṇanā vinivṛttā eṣā saṅkhyā brāhmī ca mānuṣī uktāḥ hi ete tvayā lokāḥ lokānām antareṇa ca teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā ṛṣīṇām ūrddhvaretasām sa vāyuḥ dṛṣṭa tattva arthaḥ idam tattvam uvāca ha vyaktam tarkeṇa paśyanti yogāt pratyakṣa darśinaḥ pratyāhāreṇa dhyānena tapasā ca kriyā ātmanaḥ ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāra ādyāḥ sambuddhāḥ śuddha buddhayaḥ vyapeta śokāḥ virajāḥ santaḥ brahmā iva sattamāḥ akṣayāḥ prīti saṃyuktāḥ brahme tiṣṭanti yoginaḥ ṛṣīṇām vālakhilyānām taiḥ yathā addṛtam īśvaraiḥ yathā ca eva mayā dṛṣṭam sānnidhyan tatra kurvatā an ahi asatkṛta arthānām ālayam ca īśvarasya yat īśvaraḥ paramāṇu tvāt bhāva grāhyaḥ manīṣiṇām jñānam vairāgyam aiśvaryam tapaḥ satyam kṣamā dhṛtiḥ draṣṭṛ tvam ātma sambandham adhiṣṭāna tvam eva ca avyayāni daśa etāni tasmin tiṣṭhati śaṅkare sa loka vigrahaḥ bhūtvā sāhāyyam upatiṣṭhate tasya īśvarasya yanmātra sthānam māyā mayam param māyayā kṛtam ācaṣṭe māyī devaḥ maheśvaraḥ devānām upasaṃhāraḥ tat pramāṇam hi kīrttyate eka yojana koṭī tu pañcāśat niyutāni ca ūrddhvam bhāgavata aṇḍam tu brahma lokāt param smṛtam nityāḥ hi aparisaṃkhyeyāḥ paraspara guṇa āśrayāḥ sūkṣmāḥ prasava dharmiṇyaḥ tatas prakṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ yebhyaḥ adhikarttā kṣetrajñaḥ brahma saṃjñitaḥ tāsu prakṛtimat sūkṣmam adhiṣṭātṛ tvam avyayam anutpādyam parandhāma paramāṇu pareśayam akṣayaḥ ca api anuhyaḥ ca amūrttiḥ mūrttimān asau prādurbhāvaḥ tirobhāvaḥ sthitiḥ ca eva api anugrahaḥ sa tejāḥ eṣa tamasaḥ yaḥ parastāt prakāśakaḥ bṛhatam sarvatas vṛttam īśvarāt vyavajāyata īśvarāt bīja nirbhedaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ bīje īṣyate yonim prakṛtim ācaṣṭe sā ca nārāyaṇa ātmikā purastāt brahma lokasya hi aṇḍāt arvāk ca brahmaṇaḥ śivam nāma puram tatra śaraṇam janma bhīruṇām sahasrāṇām śatam pūrṇam yojanānām dvijottamāḥ abhyantare tu vistīrṇam mahī maṇḍala saṃsthitam śātakaumbhena mahatā prākāreṇa arka varcasā dvāraiḥ caturbhiḥ sauvarṇaiḥ muktā dāma vibhūṣitaiḥ tapanīya nibhaiḥ śubhraiḥ gāḍham su kṛta veṣṭanam tat ca ākāśe puram ramyam divyam ghaṇṭā ādi nāditam sahasrāṇām śatam pūrṇam yojanānām diśaḥ daśa sahasra pādaḥ prāsādaḥ tapanīya mayaḥ śubhaḥ sphaṭikaiḥ candra saṅkāśaiḥ vaiḍhūryaiḥ soma saṃprabhaiḥ bāla sūryya prabhaiḥ ca eva sauvarṇaiḥ ca agni saṃprabhaiḥ nityāḥ hi aparisaṅkhyātāḥ paraspara guṇa āśrayāḥ tasya śākhaḥ viśākhaḥ ca naigameyaḥ ca ca aṣṭavān śrūyatām devadevasya bhaviṣya āścaryam uttamam teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā vāyuḥ vākyam jagāda ha atas param pravakṣyāmi ye tatra prati vāsinaḥ ramye pura vara śreṣṭe tasmin vaihāya bhūmiṣu nānā ratna vicitreṣu patākā bahuleṣu ca rājateṣu mahānteṣu śātakaumbha mayeṣu ca sandhyā abhra sannikāśeṣu kailāsa pratimeṣu ca iṣṭaiḥ śabda ādibhiḥ bhāgaiḥ ye bhavasya anusāriṇaḥ prāsādavara puṣpeṣu teṣu modanti suvratāḥ brahmaghoṣaiḥ aviratāḥ kathāḥ ca vividhāḥ śubhāḥ gīta vāditra ghoṣāḥ ca saṃstavāḥ ca samantataḥ saṃhatāḥ ca evam atulāḥ nānā āśraya kṛtāḥ tathā evamādīni varttante teṣām prāsāda mūrddhani sahasra pādaḥ prāsādaḥ tapanīya mayaḥ śubhaḥ sphaṭikaiḥ candra saṅkāśaiḥ vaiḍhūrya maṇi samprabhaiḥ bāla sūrya mayaiḥ ca api sauvarṇaiḥ ca agni samprabhaiḥ cukruśu ṛṣayaḥ śrutvā naimiṣeyāḥ tapasvinaḥ āpanna saṃśayāḥ ca imam vākyam ūcuḥ samīraṇam ke tu tatra mahātmānaḥ ye bhavasya anusāriṇaḥ ṛṣīṇām vacanam śrutvā vāyuḥ vākyam atha abravīt hrīmantaḥ su ūrjitāḥ dāntāḥ śaurya yuktāḥ hi a lolupāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā viśuddhena antarātmanā taiḥ labdham rudra sālokyam śāśvatam padam avyayam bhavasya rūpa sādṛśyam nītāḥ ca eva hi anuttamam vaiśvānara mukhāḥ sarve viśva rūpāḥ kaparddinaḥ nīla kaṇṭāḥ sita grīvāḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ tri locanāḥ arddhacandra kṛtaḥ aṇīṣāḥ jaṭā mukuṭa dhāriṇaḥ sarve daśa bhujāḥ vīrāḥ sugandhinaḥ taruṇa āditya saṅkāśāḥ sarve te pīta vāsasaḥ pinākapāṇayaḥ sarvve śveta govṛṣa vāhanāḥ śriyā anvitāḥ kuṇḍalinaḥ muktā hāra vibhūṣitāḥ tejasaḥ abhyadhikāḥ devaiḥ sarva jñāḥ sarva darśinaḥ vibhajya bahudhā ātmānam jarā mṛtyu vivarjitāḥ ekādaśānām rudrāṇām koṭayaḥ aneka mahātmanām bhakta anukampī bhagavān modate pārvatī priyaḥ rudrāṇām bhavasya ca mahātmanaḥ nānātvam anupaśyāmi satyam etat bravīmi vaḥ atha te ṛṣayaḥ sarve divākara sama prabhāḥ śrutvā imām paramām puṇyām kathām traiyambakīm tatas bhṛśan ca anugraham prāpya harṣam ca eva api anuttamam sambhāvayitvā ca api enām vāyum ūcuḥ mahā balam samīraṇa mahābhāga hi asmākam ca tvayā vibho tasya sthānam pramāṇam ca yathāvat parikīrttitam mahādevasya māhātmyam durvijñeyam suraiḥ api brāhma lakṣmyā svayam juṣṭā yā sā apratima śālinī mahādevasya tulyānām rudrāṇām tu mahātmanām na asti kiñcid avijñeyam anyat ca eva anugāminaḥ kim mayā ca eva vaktavyam tat vadiṣyāmi suvratāḥ ādityāḥ pāripārśveyāḥ siṃhāḥ vai krodha vikramāḥ vaiśvānarāḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ vyāghrāḥ ca eva anugāminaḥ ābhūtasaṃplave ghore sarva prāṇabhṛtām kṣaye vijñāta īśvara sadbhāvam avyaktam prabhavam tathā tatra pūrva gatāḥ teṣu kumārāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ sanakaḥ ca sanandaḥ ca tṛtīyaḥ ca sanātanaḥ voḍhuḥ ca kapilaḥ teṣām āsuriḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ muniḥ pañcaśikhaḥ ca eva ye ca anye api evamādayaḥ tatas kāle vyatikrānte kalpānām paryaye gate aneka rudra koṭyaḥ tu yāḥ prasannā maheśvarī śabda ādīn viṣayān bhogān satyasya aṣṭavidha śrayāt praviśya sarva bhūtāni jñāna yuktena tejasā vaihāya padam avyagram bhūtānām anukampayā tatra yānti mahātmānaḥ paramāṇum maheśvaram taranti su mahā varttām janma mṛtyu udakām nadīm tatas paśyanti śarvāṇam param brahmāṇam eva ca devyā vai sahitāḥ sapta yāḥ devyaḥ parikīrttitāḥ yat tat sahasram siṃhānām ādityānām tathā eva ca vaiśvānara bhūta bhavya vyāghrāḥ ca eva anugāminaḥ āveśya ātmani tān sarvān saṃkhyāya upadravān tathā lokān sapta imān sarvān mahābhūtāni pañca ca saḥ eṣaḥ otaḥ protaḥ ca bahis antar ca niścayāt ekaḥ hi bhagavān nāthaḥ hi anādiḥ ca anta kṛt dvijāḥ tatas te ṛṣayaḥ sarve divākara sama prabhāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā viśuddhena antarātmanā vrata upavāsa niratāḥ sarva bhūta dayā parāḥ yogam hi anupamam divyam prāptam taiḥ chinna saṃśayaiḥ taiḥ labdham rudra sālokyam śāśvatam padam avyayam yaḥ paṭet tapasā yuktaḥ vāyu proktām imām stutim brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vā api vaiśyaḥ vā sva kriyā paraḥ ābhūta saṃplava sthāyī hi apratīghāta lakṣaṇaḥ gāṇapatyam sa labhate sthānam vā sarvakāmikam saḥ arcyamānaḥ mahī pṛṣṭaḥ marttyānām vara daḥ bhavet iti ha uvāca bhagavān vāyuḥ vākyam idam varaḥ pratyāhāram pravakṣyāmi parasya ante svayambhuvaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sthiti kāle tu kṣīṇe tasmin tadā prabhoḥ yathā idam kurute adhyātmam su sūkṣmam viśvam īśvaraḥ avyaktān grasate vyaktam pratyāhāre ca kṛtsnaśas param tad anukalpānām apūrṇe kalpa saṅkṣaye pratyāhāre tadā tasmin bhūta tanmātra saṃkṣaye mahat ādeḥ vikārasya viśeṣa antasya saṃkṣaye āpaḥ grasanti vai pūrvvam bhūmeḥ gandha ātmakam guṇam āpaḥ tadā pranaṣṭāḥ vai vegavatyaḥ mahā svanāḥ naśyanti āpaḥ tadā ante ca rasa tanmātra saṅkṣayāt tejasā saṃhṛta rasāḥ jyotiṣṭvam prāpnuvanti uta jyotiṣaḥ api guṇam rūpam vāyuḥ anti prakāśakam pranaṣṭe rūpa tanmātre hṛta rūpaḥ vibhāvasuḥ tatas tu mūlam āsādya vāyuḥ sambhavam ātmanaḥ ūrddhvam ca adhas ca tiryak ca dodhavīti diśaḥ daśa vāyoḥ api guṇam sparśam ākāśam grasate ca tat praśāmyati tadā vāyuḥ tiṣṭhati anāvṛtam sarvam āpūrayan nādaiḥ su mahat tat prakāśate śabda mātram tat ākāśam sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati tantu bhūtādim grasate punar abhimāna ātmakaḥ hi eṣa bhūtādiḥ tāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ bhūtādim grasate ca api mahān vai buddhi lakṣaṇaḥ mahān ātmā tu vijñeyaḥ saṃkalpaḥ vyavasāyakaḥ paryāya vācakaiḥ śabdaiḥ tam āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ sampralīneṣu bhūteṣu guṇa sāmye tamaḥ maye tad ādi anta parokṣa tvāt adṛṣṭa tvāt ca kasyacid an ākhyānāt abodha tvāt ajñānāt jñāninām api anirddeśyā pravṛttiḥ vai svātmikā kāraṇe na tu yena idam āvṛtam sarvam pralīyate udaka āvaraṇam yat ca jyotiṣām līyate tu tat yat taijasam ca āvaraṇam ākāśam grasate tu tat yat vāyavyam ca āvaraṇam ākāśam grasate tu tat ākāśa āvaraṇam yat ca bhūtādiḥ grasate tu tat bhūtādim grasate ca api mahān vai buddhi lakṣaṇaḥ mahāntam grasate avyaktam guṇa sāmyam tatas param saṃhāra kārya karaṇāḥ saṃsiddhāḥ jñāninaḥ tu ye gatvā javañjavībhāve sthāneṣu eṣu prasaṃyamān pratyāhāre viyujyante kṣetrajñāḥ karaṇaiḥ punar sādharmya vaidharmma kṛta saṃyogaḥ anādimān tayoḥ evam sargeṣu vijñeyam kṣetrajñeṣu iha brāhmaṇāḥ brahma vid ca eva vijñeyaḥ kṣetra jñānāt pṛthak pṛthak viṣaya aviṣaya tvañca kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ smṛtam brahmā tu viṣayaḥ jñeyaḥ aviṣayaḥ kṣetram ucyate kṣetrajña adhiṣṭitam kṣetram kṣetrajña artham pracakṣate bahu tvāt ca śarīrāṇām śarīrī bahudhā smṛtaḥ tasmāt puruṣa nānātvam vijñeyam tu vijānatā yadā pravarttate ca eṣām bhedānām ca eva saṃyamāḥ svabhāva kāritāḥ sarve kālena mahatā tadā vinivṛtte tadā rāge sthitau ātma nivāsinām tad kāla vāsinām teṣām tadā tad doṣa darśinām utpadyate atha vairāgyam ātma vāda praṇāśanam bhojya bhoktṛ tva nānātve teṣām tad bhava darśinām pṛthak jñānena kṣetrajñāḥ tatas te brahma laukikāḥ prakṛtau karaṇāḥ nītāḥ sarve nānā pradarśinaḥ sva ātmani eva avatiṣṭhante praśāntāḥ darśana ātmakāḥ śuddhāḥ nirañjanāḥ sarve cetana acetanāḥ tathā tatra eva parinirvāṇāḥ smṛtāḥ na āgāminaḥ tu te nirguṇa tva anirātmānaḥ prakṛti ante vyatikramāt iti evam prākṛtaḥ proktaḥ pratisargaḥ svayambhuvaḥ bhidyante sarva bhūtānām karaṇāni prasaṃyame iti eṣa saṃyamaḥ ca eva tattvānām karaṇaiḥ saha dharma adharmau tapaḥ jñānam śubhe satya anṛte tathā nirindriyāṇām ca tadā jñāninām yat śubha aśubham prakṛtyām ca eva tat sarvam puṇyam pāpam pratiṣṭhati jantūnām pāpa puṇyam tu prakṛtau yat pratiṣṭitam avyakta sthāni tāni eva puṇya pāpāni jantavaḥ dharma adharmau tu jantūnām guṇa mātra ātmakau ubhau su cetanāḥ pralīyante kṣetrajña adhiṣṭitāḥ guṇāḥ rājasī tāmasī ca eva sātvikī ca eva vṛttayaḥ guṇa mātrāḥ pravarttante puruṣa adhiṣṭitāḥ tridhā ūrddhvam deva ātmakam sattvam adhobhāga ātmakam tamaḥ lokeṣu sarva bhūtānām tat na kāryam vijānatā avidyā pratyaya ārambhāḥ ārabhyante hi mānavaiḥ etāḥ tu gatayaḥ tisraḥ śubhāḥ pāpa ātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ iti ete vai trayaḥ proktāḥ bandhāḥ hi ajñāna hetukāḥ asve svam iti ca jñānam aśucau śuci niścayaḥ yeṣām ete manaḥ doṣāḥ jñāna doṣāḥ viparyyayāt rāga dveṣa nivṛttiḥ ca tat jñānam samudāhṛtam ajñānam tamasaḥ mūlam karmma dvaya phalam rajaḥ śrotra jā netra jā ca eva tvac jihvā ghrāṇataḥ tathā punarbhava karī duḥkhā karmmaṇām jāyate tu sā sa tṛṣṇaḥ abhihitaḥ bālaḥ sva kṛtaiḥ karmmaṇaḥ phalaiḥ tasmāt sthūlam anarthānām ajñānam upadiśyate tam śaktam avadhāryya ekam jñāne yatnam samācaret atas ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi rāgam bhūta apahāriṇam abhiṣaṅgāya yaḥ yasmāt viṣayaḥ api avaśa ātmanaḥ aniṣṭam abhiṣaṅgam hi prīti tāpa viṣādanam duḥkha lābhe na tāpam ca sukha anusmaraṇam tathā iti eṣa vaiṣayaḥ rāgaḥ sambhūtyāḥ kāraṇam smṛtam ajñāna pūrvakam tasmāt ajñānam tu vivarjayet yasya ca ārṣam na pramāṇam śiṣṭa ācāram tathā eva ca varṇa āśrama virodhī yaḥ śiṣṭa śāstra virodhakaḥ vividhā yātanā sthāne tiryagyonau ca ṣaḍvidhe kāraṇe viṣaye ca eva pratighātaḥ tu sarvaśas iti eṣā tāmasī vṛttiḥ bhūta ādīnām caturvidhā tattvānām ca tathā tattvam dṛṣṭvā vai tattva darśanāt sattva kṣetrajña nānātvam etat jñāna artha darśanam nānātva darśanam jñānam jñānāt vai yogam ucyate iti etat lakṣaṇam proktam samāsāt jñāna mokṣayoḥ pūrvam viyogaḥ jñānena dvitīyaḥ rāga saṃkṣayāt liṅga abhāvāt tu kaivalyam kaivatyāt tu nirañjanam tṛṣṇā kṣayāt tṛtīyaḥ tu vyākhyātam mokṣa kāraṇam nimittam apratīghāte iṣṭa śabda ādi lakṣaṇe aṣṭāvetāni rūpāṇi prākṛtāni yathākramam kṣetrajñeṣu avasajyante guṇa mātra ātmakāni tu atas urddhvam pravakṣyāmi vairāgyam doṣa darśanāt divye ca mānuṣe ca eva viṣaye pañca lakṣaṇe apradveṣaḥ anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ karttavyaḥ doṣa darśanāt tāpa prīti viṣādānām kāryantu parivarjanam evam vairāgyam āsthāya śarīrī nirmamaḥ bhavet paripavka kaṣāyaḥ hi kṛtsnān doṣān prapaśyati ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvra vāyu samīritaḥ sa śarīram upāśritya kṛtsnān doṣān ruṇaddhi vai prāṇa sthānāni bhindan hi chindan marmāṇi atītya ca sa ca ayam sarva bhūtānām prāṇa sthāneṣu avasthitaḥ samāsāt saṃvṛte jñāne saṃvṛteṣu ca karmmasu sa jīvaḥ an abhyadhiṣṭānaḥ karmmabhiḥ svaiḥ purā kṛtaiḥ aṣṭāṅga prāṇavṛttīḥ vai sa vicyāvayate punar evam prāṇaiḥ parityaktaḥ mṛtaḥ iti abhidhīyate tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu vyākhyātam mokṣa lakṣaṇam śabda ādye viṣaye doṣa viṣaye pañca lakṣaṇe a pradveṣaḥ anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ prīti tāpa vivarjanam vairāgya kāraṇam hi ete prakṛtīnām layasya ca aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ jñeyāḥ pūrva uktāḥ vai yathākramam avyakta ādyaḥ tu vijñeyāḥ bhūta antāḥ prakṛteḥ layāḥ varṇa āśrama ācāra yuktāḥ śiṣṭāḥ śāstra avirodhinaḥ varṇa āśramāṇām dharmmaḥ ayam deva sthāneṣu kāraṇam brahma ādīni piśāca antāni aṣṭau sthānāni devatāḥ aiśvaryya maṇima ādyam hi kāraṇam hi aṣṭa lakṣaṇam nimittam apratīghātaḥ iṣṭe śabda ādi lakṣaṇe aṣṭāvetāni rūpāṇi prākṛtāni yathākramam kṣetrajñeṣu anusajyante gaṇa mātra ātmakāni tu prāvṛṣ kāle pṛthaktvena paśyanti iha na cakṣuṣā paśyanti evaṃvidham siddhāḥ jīvam divyena cakṣuṣā jīva prāṇāḥ tathā liṅgam kāraṇam ca catuṣṭayam vyakta avyakte pramāṇaḥ ayam sa vai rūpam tu kṛtsnaśas avyakta anta gṛhītam ca kṣetrajña adhiṣṭitam ca yat evam jñātvā śuciḥ bhūt tvā jñānāt vai vipramucyate naṣṭam ca eva yathā tattvam tattvānām tattva darśanam bhidyate karaṇam ca api hi avyakta ajñāninaḥ tatas muktaḥ guṇa śarīreṇa prāṇa ādyena tu sarvaśas na anyat śarīram ādatte dagdhe bīje yathā aṅkuraḥ jñānāt caturddaśāt śuddhaḥ prakṛtim saḥ anuvarttate tad sadbhāvaḥ anṛtam jñeyam sadbhāvaḥ satyam ucyate a nāma rūpa kṣetrajña nāma rūpam pracakṣate yasmāt kṣetram vijānāti tasmāt kṣetrajñaḥ ucyate kṣetrajñaḥ smaryyate tasmāt kṣetram tad jñaiḥ vibhāṣyate kṣetra tva pratyayam dṛṣṭam kṣetrajñaḥ pratyayī sadā kṣayaṇāt karaṇāt ca eva kṣata trāṇāt tathā eva ca bhojya tvāt viṣaya tvāt ca kṣetram kṣetra vidaḥ viduḥ mahat ādyam viśeṣa antam sa vairūpyam vilakṣaṇam vikāra lakṣaṇam tat vai sa akṣara kṣaram eva ca tasmāt ca kāraṇāt ca eva kṣaram iti abhidhīyate akṣaram tena ca api uktam akṣīṇa tvāt tathā eva ca śuddhaḥ nirañjana ābhāsaḥ jñāna ajñāna vivarjitaḥ śuddha tvāt na tu deśyaḥ vai dṛṣṭa tvāt sama darśanaḥ yadā paśyati jñātāram śānta artham darśana ātmakam dṛśya adṛśyeṣu nirddeśyam tadā tat uddharam varam vijñātā na ca dṛśyeta pṛthaktvena iha sarvvaśas svena ātmānam tam ātmānam kāraṇa ātmā niyacchati prakṛtau kāraṇe ca eva sva ātmani eva upatiṣṭhati asti na asti iti saḥ anyaḥ vai iha amutra iti vā punar ekatvam vā pṛthaktvam vā kṣetrajña puruṣa iti vā ātmavān sa nirātmā vā cetanaḥ acetanaḥ api vā karttā vā saḥ api akarttā vā bhoktā vā bhojyam eva vā avācyam tad anākhyānāt agrāhya tvāt ahetuni kṣetrejñe nirguṇe śuddhe śānte kṣīṇe nirañjane kṣetrajña dhiṣṭitam sarvam punar sarvam pravarttate anādimān sa saṃyogaḥ mahā puruṣa jaḥ smṛtaḥ eṣā nisarga pratisarga pūrvam pradhānikī ca īśvara kāri tā ca iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ tṛtīyaḥ hetu lakṣaṇaḥ vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca bhūyas kim varttayāmi aham sūta su mahat ākhyānam bhavatā parikīrtitam prajānām manubhiḥ sārddham devānām ṛṣibhiḥ saha pitṛ gandharva bhūtānām piśāca uraga rakṣasām daityānām dānavānām ca yakṣāṇām eva pakṣiṇām tat kathyamānam asmākam bhavatā ślakṣṇayā girā manaḥ karma sukham saute prīṇāti ābhūtasambhavam evam ārādhya te sūtam satkṛtya ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ katham sūta mahā prājña punar sargaḥ prapatsyate vikāreṣu avisṛṣṭau hi avyakte ca ātmani sthite evam uktaḥ tatas sūtaḥ tadā asau lomaharṣaṇaḥ pūrvavat sa tu vijñeyaḥ samāsāt tam nibodhata dṛṣṭam ca eva anumeyam ca tarkam vakṣyāmi yuktitaḥ vikāraiḥ pratisaṃdṛṣṭe guṇa sāmye nivarttate pradhānam puruṣāṇām ca sādharmmyeṇa eva tiṣṭhati dharma adharmau pralīyete avyaktau prāṇinām sadā a buddhi pūrvam kṣetrajñaḥ adhiṣṭāsyati tān guṇān tasmāt śaraṇam avyaktam sāmye sthitvā guṇa ātmakān kṣetrajña dhiṣṭitam tat ca vaiṣamyam bhajate tu tat kṣetrajña adhiṣṭitam sattvam vikāram janayiṣyati mahat ādyam viśeṣa antam caturviṃśa guṇa ātmakam ādi devaḥ pradhānasya anugrahāya pravakṣyate pravṛtti kāle rajasā abhipanna mahat tva bhūta ādi viśeṣya tām ca viśeṣa tām ca indriya tām ca yānti guṇa avasāne patibhiḥ manuṣyāḥ ādi ante saṃprapatsyante kṣetra tajjñāḥ tu sarvaśas prasūte yā ca suvahāḥ sādhikāḥ ca api asādhikāḥ ārapsanti iha ca anyonyam vareṇa anugraheṇa ca sarve tulyāḥ prasṛṣṭa artham sarg adau yānti vikriyām guṇāḥ te yāni sarvāṇi prāk dṛṣṭeḥ pratipedire tāni eva pratipadyante sṛṣṭa mānāḥ punar punar hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharma āvṛta anṛte mahābhūteṣu nānātvam indriyārtheṣu mūrttiṣu viprayogāḥ ca bhūtānām yuṇobhyaḥ saṃpravarttate iti eṣa vaḥ mayā khyātaḥ punar sargaḥ samāsatas avyaktāt kāraṇāt tasmāt nityāt sat asat ātmakāt pradhāna puruṣābhyāntu jāyate ca maheśvaraḥ sa punar sambhāvayitā jāyate brahma saṃjñitaḥ sṛjate sa punar lokān abhimāna guṇa ātmakān ahaṅkāraḥ tu mahataḥ tasmāt bhūtāni ca ātmanaḥ vistara avayavaḥ teṣām yathāprajñam yathāśrutam kīrttitam vaḥ yathā pūrvam tathā eva abhyupadhāryyatām etat śrutvā naimiṣeyāḥ tadānīm loka utpattim saṃsthitim ca vyayan ca tasmin satre avabhṛtham prāpya śuddhāḥ puṇyam lokam ṛṣayaḥ prāpnuvanti yathā yūyam vidhivat devatā ādīn iṣṭvā ca eva avabhṛtham prāpya śuddhāḥ tyaktvā dehān āyuṣaḥ ante kṛtārthān puṇyān lokān prāpya yatheṣṭam cariṣyatha ete te naimiṣeyāḥ vai iṣṭvā sṛṣṭvā ca vai tadā jagmuḥ ca avabhṛdha snātāḥ svargam sarve tu satriṇaḥ viprāḥ tathā yūyam api ca iṣṭvā bahuvidhaiḥ makhaiḥ āyuṣaḥ ante tatas svargam gantāraḥ stha dvijottamāḥ anuṣaṅgaḥ upodvātaḥ upasaṃhāraḥ eva ca evam etat catuṣpādam purāṇam loka sammatam uvāca bhagavān sākṣāt vāyuḥ loka hite rataḥ prādhānikīm imām sṛṣṭim tathā eva īśvara kāritām idam yaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vidvān itihāsam purātanam śrṛṇuyāt śrāvayet vā api tathā adhyāpayate api ca sthāneṣu sa mahā indrasya modate śāśvatīḥ samāḥ teṣām kīrttimatām kīrttim prajā īśānām mahātmanām prathayan pṛthivīśānām brahma bhūyāya gacchati dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam puṇyam vedaiḥ ca sammatam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanena uktam purāṇam brahma vādinā manvantara īśvarāṇām ca yaḥ kīrtim prathayet imām devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca bhūri draviṇa tejasām yaḥ ca idam śrāvayet vidvān sadā parvaṇi parvaṇi yaḥ ca idam śrāvayet śrāddhe brāhmaṇān pādam antatas akṣayam sārvakāmīyam pitṝn tat ca upatiṣṭhati yasmāt purā hi ananti idam purāṇam tena ca ucyate tathā eva triṣu varṇeṣu ye manuṣyāḥ pradhānataḥ yāvanti asya śarīreṣu romakūpāṇi sarvaśas sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām divi modate sarvva pāpa haram puṇyam pavitram ca yaśasvi ca brahmā dadau śāstram idam purāṇam mātariśvane tasmāt ca uśanasā prāptam tasmāt ca api bṛhaspatiḥ savitā mṛtyave prāha mṛtyuḥ ca indrāya vai punar indraḥ ca api vasiṣṭāya saḥ api sārasvatāya ca śaradvataḥ triviṣṭāya saḥ antarikṣāya dattavān varṣiṇe ca āntarikṣaḥ vai saḥ api trayyāruṇāya ca trayyāruṇaḥ dhanañjaye sa ca prādāt kṛtañjaye kṛta ñjayāt tṛṇañjayaḥ bharadvājāya saḥ api atha sa dadau somaśūṣmāya sa dadau tṛṇabindave tṛṇabinduḥ tu dakṣāya dakṣaḥ provāca śaktaye śakteḥ parāśaraḥ ca api garbha sthaḥ śrutavān idam parāśarāt jātukarṇaḥ tasmāt dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ dvaipāyanāt punar ca api mayā prāptam dvijottamāḥ iti eva vācā brahma ādi guruṇā samudāhṛtā dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam puṇyam sarva artha sādhakam pāpa ghnam niyamena idam śrotavyam brāhmaṇaiḥ sadā na aśucau na api pāpāya na api a saṃvatsara uṣite na a śraddadhāna a viduṣe na a putrāya kathañcana vahnim vakram candra sūryau ca netre diśaḥ śrotre ghrāṇam āhuḥ ca vāyum vāyo vedān ca antarikṣam śarīram kṣitim pādau tārakāḥ romakūpān tam deva devam jananam janānām sarvveṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭitam ca varam varāṇām vara dam maheśvaram brahmāṇam ādim prayataḥ namasye akṣaram paramam brahma paramātmā param padam atas ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi gayāmāhātmyam uttamam yojanānām sa pādam ca śatam tasya ucchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ stha me devāḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ āsīt dharmmaḥ mahā tejāḥ sarvva vijñāna pāragaḥ brahmaṇaḥ mānasaḥ putraḥ marīciḥ nāma viśrutaḥ mataṅgasya padam tatra dṛśyate sarva mānuṣaiḥ mataṅgasya padam tatra dṛśyate sarva mānuṣaiḥ gayāyām ca akṣayam śrāddham japa homa tapāṃsi ca mātā pitāmahī ca eva tathā eva prapitāmahī atra snātaḥ divam yāti sva śarīreṇa mānavaḥ ātmānam tārayet sadyas daśa pūrvān daśa aparān gayāyām dharmmapṛṣṭe ca sarasi pitṝn pitāmahān ca eva tathā eva prapitāmahān tatra snātaḥ divam yāti sva śarīreṇa mānavaḥ tat paṅgaja vanam puṇyam puṇya kṛdbhiḥ niṣevitam
